modalanE  nuDiyannu  makkaLu  halavu  hantagaLa  mUlaka
kaliyabEkAguttade.  I  ellA  hantagaLannU  avaru  tAvAgiyE
dATuttA  munduvariyuttAre.  yAva  maguvU  I  hantagaLannu
dATadiruvudilla.

idE rItiyalli, eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyallU halavu hanta
gaLiruttave, mattu kelavu makkaLu, kalisuvike aSTu cannAgilladiddarU,
avellavannU dATi munde hOguttAre. Adare, bEre kelavu makkaLu
yAvudAdarU ondu hantadalli silukikonDiruttAre, mattu allinda
munde hOguvudu hEgendu tiLiyade, allE uLiyuttAre. idu
modalanE nuDiya kalikegU eraDanE nuDiya kalikegU naDuviruva
innondu vyatyAsa.

7.1.3 makkaLa kalike mattu doDDavara kalike
eraDanE  nuDiyannu  makkaLu  SAleyalli  kaliyuvudakkU,  baLika
doDDavarAda mEle kAlEjinalli, illavE adakkU munde ondu
kelasadalliruvAga kaliyuvudakkU naDuve halavu vyatyAsagaLive:

makkaLiginta  doDDavarige  heccu  tiLuvaLikeyiruttade.  tamma
mundiruva sangatigaLannu biDisinODi, avugaLa oLaguTTannu tiLidu
koLLaballantaha aLavu avaralli cikkavariginta hecciruttade. I aLavannu
avaru tamma eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyallU baLasikoLLaballaru.

tAvu IgAgalE kalitiruva modalanE nuDigU Iga kaliyuttiruva
eraDanE  nuDigU  naDuve  sollarimeya  kaTTalegaLalli  entaha
vyatyAsagaLella ive embudara tiLivannu cikkavariginta doDDavaru heccu
cannAgi  tamma  kalikeyalli  baLasikoLLaballaru.  hAgAgi,  eraDanE
nuDiyannu kalisuvavaru cikkavarigintalU doDDavarige sollarimeya
kaTTalegaLannu nEravAgi tiLisabahudu.

idallade,  nuDiya  kalikeyalli  eraDu  mukya  hantagaLiruttave:
dinabaLakege bEkAguva mAtugaLannu salIsAgi nuDiyalu kaliyuvudu
ondu  hanta,  mattu  gaNita,  vijnAna  modalAda  viSayagaLannu
tiLidukoLLuvudakkAgi, mattu hAge tiLidukonDudannu innobbarige
vivarisi hELuvudakkAgi, nuDiyannu baLasalu kaliyuvudu innondu

I eraDu hantagaLa naDuvina mukya vyatyAsavEnendare, modalanE
hantadalli nuDiya baLakege kaysanne, kaNNusanne, mAtina EriLita modalA
davugaLa neravu siguttade. Adare, eraDanE hantada kalikeyalli nAvu
paDeyabEkAgiruva huruLugaLannella pada mattu sollugaLannu mAtravE
gamanisi paDeyabEkAguttade.

eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruva makkaLige adaralli modalanE
hantavannu talapalu eraDu varSagaLu sAkAgabahudu; Adare, eraDanE
hantavannu talapabEkiddalli avarige ArELu varSagaLE bEkAgabahudu.
makkaLa manassu sAkaSTu beLavaNigeyannu paDeyuvallivarege avarige
I eraDanE hantavannu talapalu baruvudilla. hAgAgi, I eraDanE

hantada kalikeyannu cikkavarigintalU doDDavaru heccu cannAgi mattu
heccu bEgane naDesaballaru.

Adare,  bEre  halavu  viSayagaLalli  doDDavaru  tamma  eraDanE
nuDiya kalikeyalli cikkavariginta tumbA hinde bILuttAre. ettugegAgi,
tamma modalanE nuDiyalli baLakeyAgilladantaha hosa uligaLu
eraDanE  nuDiyalli  baLakeyAguttiveyAdare,  antaha  uligaLa
ulipannu (uccAraNeyannu) cikkavaraSTu sulabavAgi mattu cennAgi
doDDavaru kalitukoLLalAraru.

yAkendare, uligaLa naDuvina vyatyAsavannu mAtinalli baLasikoLLuva
kasuvu makkaLalliruva hAge doDDavaralliruvudilla. hosa uligaLannu
horaDisuva  kasuvU  avara  nAligeyalli  uLidiruvudilla.  tAvu
kaliyuttiruva eraDanE nuDiyannu tAynuDiyAgi ADuvavara hAge
ADalu doDDavarigintalU cikka makkaLu heccu suLuvAgi kalitukoLLa
ballaru.

idallade, bEreyU halavu viSayagaLalli doDDavara niluvu gaTTi
gonDiddu, badalAvaNegaLige hondikoLLalu avarige kaSTavAguttade.
eraDanE  nuDiyannu  kalitukoLLuvavaru  tamma  niluvinalli  halavu
bageya badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLabEkAguvudarinda, I kelasavannu
doDDavariginta cikkavaru heccu suLuvAgi mADaballaru.

cikka makkaLu eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruvAga tappu mADalu
hedaruvudilla. hAgAgi, avarige kalikeyalli bEgane munde hOgalu
baruttade. Adare, doDDavaru tappu mADidare yArAdarU nagabahudu
embudAgi  hedaruttiruttAre.  avarige  kalisuvavaru  avariginta
cikkavarAgiddare,  avaru  tappu  mADalu  innaSTu  hedaruttAre.  I
hedarikeyE avarannu kalikeyalli hinde bILuva hAge mADuttade.

7.2 eraDanE nuDiyAgi ingliSna kalike
ingliS nuDiyannu (illavE hindi, phrenc, jarmannantaha bErondu
nuDiyannu) kaliyuttiruva kannaDada makkaLige mattu doDDavarige kannaDada

sollarimeyinda neravEnAdarU dorakaballudE embudannu keLage
(7.2-5)ralli oredu nODalAgide.

7.2.1 tAynuDiyannu kalikeyinda horagiDuvudu
SAleyalli ingliS nuDiyannu eraDanE nuDiyAgi kalisuttiruvAga
makkaLa tAynuDiyannu baLasabahudE illavE baLasabEkE emba viSaya
dalli ittIcege tumbA carcegaLu naDeyuttive; Adare, ivattu heccina
arivigarU ingliS nuDiya kalikeyalli tAynuDiya baLake halavu
bageyalli neravAgaballudu embudannu oppuva hantakke bandiddAre.
idakke modalu, ingliS taragatigaLalli tAynuDiyannu baLasalE
kUDadu emba kaTTaleyondu kaLeda SatamAnadalli beLedubandittu.
tAynuDiyannu  baLasidalli  adu  ingliS  kalikege  aDDiyannunTu
mADuttadeyemba tappu tiLivaLike idakke mukyavAda kAraNavAgittu.
idallade, makkaLu yAvAgalU ingliS nuDiyannE kELuttiddalli,
mattu bEre yAva nuDiyannU kELadiddalli, avarige ingliSnalli
tumbA  cannAgi  mattu  bahaLa  bEgane  mAtanADalu  bandItemba
anisikeyU idakke kAraNavAgittu.

ingliS nuDiyannu kalikeya nuDiyAgi baLasuva kelavu SAlegaLa
llantU  makkaLu  SAleyoLage  tamma  tAynuDiyannu  baLasuvudE
aparAdavembudAgi ivattigU parigaNisalAguttide.

nijakkU idu makkaLa illavE doDDavara kalike hEge sAguttade
embudannu  ariyade  mADiruvantaha  kaTTale.  yArE  Agali,
tammalliruva tiLuvaLikeya taLahadiya mEle hosa tiLuvaLikeyannu
paDeyabEkAguttade.  SAlege  baruva  modalE  makkaLu  tamma
tAynuDiyalli cannAgi mAtanADalu kalitiruttAre. tamma anisikegaLannu
A  nuDiyalli  tiLisuvudu  hEge,  mattu  adaralli  bEreyavaru
hELidudannu  kELi  tiLiyuvudu  hEge  embudannu  avaru  cannAgi
tiLidiruttAre.  avara  AlOcanegaLellavU  A  nuDiyalliyE
naDeyuttiruttave.

hAgiruvAga, makkaLu SAleyalli hosa nuDiyondannu kaliya
bEkiddalli, adannu avaru adakke modalE kalitukonDidda tAynuDiya
mUlakavEnE  kaliyabEku.  idallade,  nuDiya  svarUpaventahadu
embudannu SAlege sEruva modalEnE avarige tAynuDiya kalike
tiLisikoTTide. uligaLannu baLasi padagaLannu unTumADuvudu hEge,
avannu baLasi padakantegaLannu mattu sollugaLannu unTumADuvudu
hEge, avu huruLugaLannu hEge sUcisaballuvu embudannella avaru
adakke modalE tamma tAynuDiya kalikeya mUlaka tiLidiruttAre.
avaru kaliyabEkAgiruva hosa nuDiyalli (ingliSnalli) idannE
bErondu bageyalli naDesalAguttade. I bage entahadu embudannu
avaru gamanisuva hAge mADuva mUlaka, adannu kaliyalu toDagisu
vudE  sariyAda  mattu  suLuvAda  dAri.  I  rIti  tAynuDiya
mUlaka hosa nuDiyannu kalisahoraTalli, makkaLige nemmadiya kalike
dorakuttade,  mattu  hosa  nuDiyalli  anjade  mAtu  kaliyalu
baruttade.

idakke badalu, tAynuDiyannu SAleyalli baLasalE kUDademba
kaTTaleyannu mADidalli, kalikeyalli avaru baLasaballa ondu amUlya
vAda  sAdanavannu  avarinda  kittukonDahAgAguttade,  mattu
tAynuDiya  kuritAgi  avaralli  kILarimeyannu  unTumADida
hAgAguttade.  idarindAgi,  halavu  makkaLige  tamma  tannatanavannE
kaLedukonDa hAgeyU Aguttade.

nijakkU makkaLu tamma eraDanE nuDiyannu modalanE nuDiya
taLahadiya  mElEnE  kaliyuttAre.  taragatiyalli  tAynuDiyannu
baLasabArademba kaTTaleyannu mADidarU avaru kaliyuttiruvAga
manassinalli illavE miduLinalli tAynuDiyannu baLasadiruvudilla.
yAkendare,  hAge  baLasadiralu  avarige  sAdyavE  illa!  hAgAgi,
avara  tAynuDiyannu  manassinalli  mAtravE  baLasalAguttideyO
illavE horagU baLasalAguttideyO embudE illiruva vyatyAsa.
pada  mattu  sollugaLigU  avugaLa  huruLigU  naDuviruva
pattuge(sambanda)yannu  tiLidukonDu,  adannu  nenapinalli

uLisikoLLuva  kelasa  makkaLa  miduLina  ondu  kaDeyalli  mAtra
naDeyuttade.  hosadondu  nuDiyannu  kaliyuva  makkaLallU  I
kelasa adE jAgadalli, endare avaru tamma tAynuDiyannu kaliyu
ttiruvAga  baLasida  jAgadallE  naDeyuttade.  eraDanE  nuDiyannu
enTu-hattu  varSa  dATida  makkaLu  kaliyuttiruvAgalU  avara
miduLinalli  I  kelasavannu  naDesalu  bEre  hosa  jAga  baLakege
baruvudilla.  endare,  tAynuDiya  tiLivige  sambandisida  hAgEnE
avara eraDanE nuDiya tiLivu miduLinalli nelegoLLuttade.

7.2.2 kaTTaLeya mUla
sumAru eraDu sAvira varSagaLindalU makkaLige (illave doDdavarige)
eraDanE nuDiyannu tAynuDiya taLahadiya mElEnE kalisalAgu
ttittu. ettugegAgi, lyATin, grIk modalAda nuDigaLannu kalisuvavaru
avugaLa sollarimeya (vyAkaraNada) kaTTalegaLannu mattu avugaLa
pada, padakante, sollu modalAdavugaLa huruLugaLannu tAynuDi
yallEnE kalisuttiddaru. namma dESadalli samskrutada kalikeyU heccu
kaDime idE rItiyallE naDeyuttittu.

I holabannu (paddatiyannu) biTTukoTTu, halavu bageya hosa
holabugaLannu  mukyavAgi  ippattanE  SatamAnadalli  baLakege
taralAyitu.  ivugaLalli  heccinavannU  ingliS,  jarman,  phranc
modalAda nuDigaLannu yurOpinalli bEre nuDigaLannADuvavarige
avara  eraDanE  nuDiyAgi  kalisuvalli  baLakege  taralAyitu.  I
eraDanE nuDiya taragatigaLalli halavu nuDigaLannu tAynuDiyAgi
baLasuva kaligariddarAda kAraNa, mattu avarige eraDanE nuDiyannu
kalisuvavaru avugaLalli heccendare onderaDannu mAtravE tiLididdarAda
kAraNa,  kalikeyinda  tAynuDiyannu  horagirisuvudE  avarige
(kalisuvavarige, kaliyuvavarigalla!) anukUlavAda holabAgittu.
hAgAgi, ippattanE SatamAnadalli baLakege bandidda heccina holabu
gaLallU tAynuDiya baLakeyannu eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyinda dUra
irisalAyitu. Adare, taragatiya makkaLellarU ondE tAynuDiyannu

paDediruva illavE ondE nuDiyannu tiLidiruva nammallina ingliS
taragatigaLallU idE holabannu anusarisuttiruvudu mAtra tIra
vicitravAgide. adu mElina holabugaLa kuruDu anukaraNeyAgide.
modalanE  nuDiyannu  baLasade  eraDanE  nuDiyannu  nEravAgi
kalisatoDagidAga, kelavu makkaLige heccu tondareyAguvudilla. avaru
suLuvAgi  kalikeyalli  munde  hOguttAre.  Adare  bEre  kelavu
makkaLige idu tumbA toDakina kelasavendenisuttade. hAgAgi, avaru
kalikeyalli hinde bILuttAre.

antaha makkaLige kalikeya modala hantagaLalli tAynuDiya neravannu
koTTalli, avaru bEgane kalikeyalli munde hOgaballaru. AmEle,
hAge munde hOguttiddante, tAynuDiya neravannu kaDime mADuttA
hOgabahudu.

ingliS  padagaLa  huruLannu  tiLisuvalli,  adara  sollarimeya
kaTTalegaLannu vivarisi hELuvalli, mattu makkaLige kalikeyalli toDaku
gaLEnAdarU iddalli avu entahavu embudannu tiLidukoLLuvalli
avara  tAynuDi  neravige  baraballudu.  nijakkU  intaha  kaDegaLalli
halavu mandi kalisugaru ivattU taragatigaLalli makkaLa tAynuDiyannu
baLasuttiruttAre; Adare, hAge baLasuttiruvAga tAvEnO ondu
doDDa tappannu mADuttiddEve emba anisike avaralliruttade.

ingliS taragatigaLalli tAynuDiyannu baLasalEbArademba kaTTale
yannu tegedu hAkidalli, intaha tappanisike kalisuvavaralli illavAgu
ttade, mattu kaliyuva makkaLigU tamma manassinoLagEnE naDesuttidda
kelasavannu horage taragatiyallU hedarikeyillade naDesalu baruttade.
idarindAgi  avarige  tamma  tAynuDiya  mEle  kILarimeyU
beLeyuvudilla.

7.2.3 tAynuDiya sollarimeya baLake
eraDanE  mahAyuddada  samayadalli  amerikAda  paDeyALugaLige
raSyan,  japAnIs,  jarman  modalAda  horanADina  nuDigaLannu

bahaLa  bEgane,  endare  kelavE  kelavu  vAragaLalli  kalisuvudakkAgi
nuDiyarigara (bASAvijnAnigaLa) morehogalAyitu. I kelasavannu
naDesuvudakkAgi  avaru  A  nuDigaLalli  baLakeyAguva  halavAru
sollarimeya kaTTalegaLannu kanDuhiDidaru, mattu avannu nuDigaLa
kalisuvikeyalli tumbA cennAgi baLasalu kalitaru.

intaha  kalisuvikeyalli  ingliS  nuDiya  (tAynuDiya)
sollarimegU  kalisabEkAgiruva  eraDanE  nuDiya  sollarimegU
naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLannu baLasikonDalli kalike innaSTu vEgavAgi
sAguttade  embudannu  avaru  kanDukonDaru,  mattu  adakkAgi
eraDeraDu  nuDigaLa  sollarimegaLannu  hOlisi  tOrisuvantaha
hOlikeya  sollarimegaLannu  tayArisatoDagidaru.  AmEle,
intaha sollarimegaLannu halavAru nuDijODigaLigAgi tayArisa
lAyitu,  mattu  avugaLa  mEle  halavu  pustakagaLannU  horatara
lAyitu.

Adare AmEle, nuDigaLa sollarimeya kuritAgi comskI avara
siddAntagaLu mandimeccuge paDedAga, adakke hinde naDedidda halavAru
arakegaLu mUlegumpAduvu. idakke kAraNavEnendare, A arakegaLella
mukyavAgi manuSyana naDavaLikeya mEle (avanu entaha sollugaLannu
nuDiyuttAne embudara mEle) avalambisidduvu. nuDiya mElina
arakege  manuSyana  naDavaLikegintalU  Atana  oLagina  (manassina)
arimeyE AdAravAgirabEkembudAgi comskI tOrisikoTTiddaru.
idarindAgi,  manuSyara  naDavaLikeya  mEle  avalambisidda  nuDi
yarimeya (mattu sollarimeya) siddAntagaLellavU mandimeccuge
yannu kaLedukonDuvu.

I rIti mUlegumpAdavugaLalli eraDanE nuDiya kalisuvikeyalli
sAkaSTu pariNAmakAriyAgidda mEle vivarisidantaha hOlikeya
sollarimegaLU sEridduvu.

idE samayadalli, makkaLu modalanE nuDiyannu (tAynuDiyannu)
kaliyuva hAgeyE eraDanE nuDiyannU tAvAgiyE kaliyaballaru;
hAgAgi, modalanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruva makkaLa hAge eraDanE

nuDiyannu kaliyuvavarU A ondu nuDiyannu mAtravE yAvAgalU
kELuttiruva hAge mattu Oduttiruva hAge mADidalli, modalanE
nuDiyannu kalitaSTE vEgadalli avaru eraDaneyadannU tAvAgiyE
kalitAru; avarige sollarimeyannu kalisabEkAgiyE illa embudAgi
vAdisalAyitu.

Adare mEle sUcisida hAge, ittIcege naDesida arakegaLu I
vAda  tappAdudu  embudannu  tOrisikoTTive.  nijakkU  eraDanE
nuDiya kalike modalanE nuDiya kalikeya hAge naDeyalu sAdyavE
illa.  yAkendare,  modalanE  nuDiyannu  kaliyuva  samayadalli
makkaLa miduLu nuDiya maTTige baridAgiruttade. antaha baridAgiruva
miduLinalli  avaru  ondu  nuDiyannu  hosadAgi  mUDisikoLLa
bEkAgide.

idakke badalu, eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuva samayadalli avara
miduLu  A  rIti  baridAgiruvudilla.  adaralli  modalanE  nuDi
nelenintiruttade.  hAgAgi,  eraDanE  nuDiyannu  kaliyahoraDuva
makkaLalliruva  I  amUlyavAda  sAdanavannu  baLasade  eraDaneya
nuDiyannu  kaliyuva  hAge  avarannu  ottAyisuvudu  nijakkU
peddutanavallade bErEnalla.

idallade, makkaLa tAynuDiya sollarimegU avaru kaliyuttiruva
eraDanE nuDiya sollarimegU naDuve iruva mukya vyatyAsagaLannu
avara  gamanakke  tandalli,  avara  kalike  bEgane  munde  sAguttade
embudannu  ittIcegina  kelavu  arakegaLu  tOrisikoTTive.  kelavu
makkaLu  intaha  sollarimeya  tiLuvaLikeyannu  koDisadiddarU
kalikeyalli munde hOgaballaru. Adare, kalikeyalli hinde bILuva
bEre kelavu makkaLige sollarimeya tiLivannu koDisidalli avarU
munde hOgaballaru.

7.2.4 kalikeya tappugaLu
eraDanE  nuDiya  kalikeyinda  modalanE  nuDiyannu  dUra
irisabEkendu hELuvudakke innondu kAraNavannU koDalAguttade.

adEnendare, eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli makkaLa modalanE nuDi
talehAkuttade; eraDanE nuDiyalli sollugaLannu kaTTuvAga, adara
kaTTalegaLannu  baLasuva  badalu,  makkaLu  tamma  modalanE  nuDiya
kaTTalegaLannu  baLasahOguttAre.  idarindAgi  avara  kalikeyalli
tappugaLu  talehAkuttave.  intaha  tappugaLu  bArada  hAge  nODi
koLLalu,  eraDanE  nuDiyannu  kaliyuva  samayadalli  makkaLa
tAynuDiyannu  kalikeyinda  dUra  irisuvudE  sariyAda  dAri
embudAgi avaru vAdisuttAre.

Adare, eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruvAga makkaLu mADuva
tappugaLalli heccinavU tappugaLE alla embudAgi ittIcegina arakegaLu
tOrisikoTTive. makkaLu tamma eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyannu halavu
hantagaLalli  naDesuttAre,  mattu  ondondu  hantadallU  avaru
adaradE Ada sollarimeya kaTTalegaLannu baLasuttiruttAre.

eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruva makkaLa mAtinalli kANisuva
tappugaLalli heccinavU I rIti kaliyabEkAgiruva nuDigU avariruva
kalikeya hantada nuDigU naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLannu sUcisuttavallade
nijakkU avu tappugaLalla. makkaLu kalikeya ondu hantadinda innondu
hantakke  dATuttiruvante I vyatyAsagaLu tAvAgiyE illavAguttave.
idallade, avaru I hantagaLannu dATuva modalE avakke sambandisida
tappu(vyatyAsa)gaLannu illavAgisalU baruvudilla.

tAynuDiya kayvADadindAgiyU eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli
kelavu  tappugaLu  kANisikoLLaballuvEnO  nija.  Adare,  ivannu
hOgalADisuvudakkAgi tAynuDiyannu kalikeyinda dUra irisuvudu
sariyAda dAriyalla. sAmAnyavAgi eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuvavaru
modalige tamma modalanE nuDiya kaTTalegaLannE adarallU baLasalu
hOguttAre.  Adare  AmEle,  eraDanE  nuDiyalli  sariyAda
sollugaLannu unTumADuvalli A kaTTalegaLu sOtuhOguvudannu
kanDukonDu,  adaravE  Ada  kaTTalegaLannu  baLasalu  kaliyuttAre.
I ellA kelasagaLU avara miduLinalli tiLivige eTakada rUpadalli
naDeyuttiruttave.

kelavarige I kelasavannu tAvAgiyE suLuvAgi naDesalu baruttade,
Adare  bEre  kelavarige  idannu  tAvAgiyE  naDesalu  baruvudilla.
antaha makkaLige modalanE nuDiya kaTTalegaLu entahavu, mattu
eraDanE nuDiya kaTTalegaLu avugaLinda yAva rItiyalli bErAgive
embudannu tOrisikoTTalli, I kelasavannu naDesalu avarige heccu
suLuvAguttade embudannu ittIcege kanDukoLLalAgide.

eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli tAynuDiyinda tondare mAtravallade
neravU  dorakuttade  embudannU  illi  gamanisuvudu  avaSya.
tAynuDiyannu eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyinda dUra irisabEkendu
hELuvavaru  adarinda  unTAguva  tondareya  kaDege  mAtravE
gamana  harisiddArallade,  adarinda  sigaballa  neravina  kaDege  gamana
harisilla.  nijakkU  eraDanE  nuDiya  kalikeyalli  tAynuDiyannu
baLasuvudarindAguva  tondaregintalU  adannu  kaDegaNisu
vudarindAguva tondareyE heccu keDukannunTumADaballudu.

7.2.5 Odalu-bareyalu kaliyuvudu
makkaLige eraDanE nuDiyalli Odalu mattu bareyalu hEge kalisabEku
embudara kuritu ittIcege halavu arakegaLannu naDesalAgide. Odalu
mattu bareyalu modalige avara tAynuDiyalli kalisi, AmEle
eraDanE nuDiyalli kalisuvudu oLLeyadE, illavE modaligEnE
nEravAgi eraDaneya nuDiyalli kalisuvudu oLLeyadE embudu
intaha arakegaLa mundidda ondu kELvi.

makkaLu eraDanE nuDiginta tamma tAynuDiyalli heccu suLuvAgi
Odalu mattu bareyalu kaliyaballaru, mattu hAge kalita mEle A
kelasagaLannu naDesuvudakkAgi tamma tAynuDiyalli kalitiruva caLakagaLalli
heccinavannU avaru eraDanE nuDigU suLuvAgi mAreDegoLisaballaru
embudannu I arakegaLu kanDukonDive. hAgAgi, makkaLige Odu-
barahavannu modalige avara tAynuDiyallEnE kalisi, AmEle avara
eraDanE  nuDiyalli  Odu-barahavannu  kalisuvudu  oLLeyademba
tIrmAnakke baralAgide.

kannaDigara maTTige hELuvudAdare, makkaLu Odalu kaliyuva kelasa
vannu eraDanE nuDiyAda ingliSnalli naDesuvudakkinta modalu
kannaDadalli naDesuvudu oLLeyadu embudakke bErondu mukyavAda
kAraNavide. kannaDadalli barige(akSara)gaLigU ulikantegaLigU (mattu
uligaLigU) naDuve nEravAda hondANikeyide. (idakke samskrutadinda
eravalAgi paDeda padagaLu mAtra - avannu samskrutadalliruva hAgeyE
bareyabEkemba anavaSyakavAda kaTTaLeyiruva kAraNa - horapaDike
(apavAda)gaLAgive.) hAgAgi, kannaDa padagaLannu mAtravE baLasiruva
barahagaLa mUlaka (illavE hosa barahavannu baLasiruva barahagaLa
mUlaka) makkaLige kannaDadalli tumbA suLuvAgi Odalu kalisabahudu.
ingliSnalli tumbA toDaku toDakAda spelling samasyeyide.
hAgAgi,  adara  barahagaLalli  barigegaLigU  uligaLigU  naDuve
hondANike ide embudannu makkaLu gamanisuva hAge mADuvudu
tumbA toDakina kelasa. halavu mandi makkaLa gamanakke idu baruvudE
illa.  hAgAgi,  antaha  makkaLu  padagaLannu  barigegaLAgi  oDedu
uligaLondige hondisalu hOgade nEravAgi Odalu toDaguttAre.
I rIti Odalu modalige aSTondu tondareyAguvudillavAdarU,
Odinalli munde hOdante heccu heccu barahagaLannu OdabEkAguvu
dAda kAraNa, avaru Odinalli hinde bILatoDaguttAre (2.3 nODi).
hAgAgi, modalige kannaDadalli Odalu kaliyuva mUlaka sariyAgi
Oduva bage hEge embudannu tiLidukonDiruva makkaLu ingliSnallU
sariyAgi Odalu suLuvAgi kalitukoLLaballaru. yAkendare, Oduva
kelasakkAgi kannaDadalli paDediruva caLakavannu avaru suLuvAgi tamma
ingliS OdigU mAreDegoLisaballaru.

Odalu kaliyuvudakkintalU bareyalu kaliyuvudu heccu toDakina
kelasa. idannu eraDanE nuDiyalli naDesalu kaliyuvudu mattaSTu
toDakina kelasa. I eraDanE kelasavannu tamma tAynuDiyalli bareyalu
kalitiruva makkaLu heccu suLuvAgi naDesaballaru. yAkendare, avaru
idakkAgi tamma tAynuDiyalli kalitukonDidda caLakagaLalli heccinavannU
eraDanE nuDiya baravaNigegU mAreDegoLisaballaru.

makkaLige  tamma  tAynuDiyalli  AlOcisalu  EnU  tondare
yAguvudilla. Adare, eraDanE nuDiyalli sAkaSTu paLaguvallivarege
avarige adaralli AlOcisalu baruvudilla. hAgAgi, bareyabEkA
giruva viSayagaLannu modalige tAynuDiyalli AlOcisi, mattu
avannu bEkAda kramadalli sAvagisi(jODisi)konDu, AmEle eraDanE
nuDiyalli bareyuvudu avarige heccu suLuvAda kelasavAgaballudu.
idallade, tAynuDiyalli bareyalu kalitiruva makkaLu tAvu oTTu
gUDisiruva viSayagaLannu modalige tamma tAynuDiyalli baredu,
AmEle adannu eraDanE nuDige nuDimAra(bASAntarisa)bahudu.
eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuva modala hantagaLalli intaha nuDi
mArikeya  baLakeyU  neravige  baruttadeyendu  ittIcegina  kelavu
arakegaLu tOrisikoTTive.

eraDanE nuDiyannu kaliyuttiruvAga oTToTTige tamma tAynuDi
yallU  Odu-barahada  tiLivannu  heccisikoLLuva  makkaLu  eraDanE
nuDiya kalikeyalli bEre makkaLiginta munde hOguttAre. tAynuDi
yannu pUrti kaDegaNisiruva makkaLu modamodalige tumbA vEgavAgi
munde hOguttiruvante kANisuttAre; Adare, AmEle halavu makkaLu
tamma eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli hinde bILatoDaguttAre. idarinda
gottAguvudEnendare,  eraDanE  nuDiya  kalikeyalli  tAynuDiya
bembala heccina makkaLigU bEkAguttade.

illi innondu viSayavannU gamanisabEkAgide. mEle sUcisida
hAge, nuDiya kalikeyalli eraDu hantagaLiruttave. adaralli salIsAgi
mAtanADalu kaliyuvudu ondu hanta mattu gaNita, vijnAna moda
lAda viSayagaLannu tiLiyalu mattu innobbarige tiLisalu kaliyuvudu
innondu hanta.

SAleyalli modalinindalU ingliS nuDiyannE kalikenuDiyAgi
baLasiruva makkaLu A nuDiyalli salIsAgi mAtanADuvudannu gamani
siruva halavarige, avaru adannu bahaLa cannAgi kalitukonDiddArendu
anisuttade. hAgAgi, tamma makkaLU ingliS nuDiyannE kalikenuDi
yAgi  baLasi,  AdaSTu  bEgane  A  nuDiyalli  pariNatarAgabEkendu

avaru bayasuttAre. Adare, nijakkU antaha makkaLu tamma ingliS
kalikeyalli modalaneya hantavannaSTE talapiruttAre.

munde  eraDanE  hantavannu  talapuva  kelasadalli  avaru  hinde
bILuttAre. idakke kAraNavEnendare, makkaLu tamma tAynuDiyalli
I kelasavannu heccu suLuvAgi naDesaballaru, mattu AmEle adannu
tamma eraDaneya nuDigU suLuvAgi mAreDegoLisa(vargAyisa)ballaru.
ingliS nuDiyannu kalikenuDiyAgi baLasuttiruva makkaLige intaha
tAynuDiya neravu dorakuvudillavAda kAraNa, avarige tamma kalikeya
eraDanE hantavannu talapuvalli tondareyAguttade.

hAgAgi, modalige kannaDavannE kalikenuDiyAgi baLasi, AmEle
hayskUlnalli, illavE munde kAlEjinalli ingliS nuDiyannu
kalikenuDiyAgi baLasuva makkaLu A nuDiyalli eraDanE hantavannu
talapuvalli suruvinindalU adakkAgi ingliS nuDiyannE baLasuva
makkaLiginta munde hOguttAre.

7.2.6 doDDavara kalike
eraDanE nuDiyondannu makkaLu SAlegaLalli kaliyuvudakkU doDDava
rAda mEle kAlEjinalli, illavE munde kelasadalliruvAga kaliyuvu
dakkU  naDuve  halavu  vyatyAsagaLiveyembudannu  nAvu  mEle
(7.1.3)ralli nODiruvevu. doDDavara kalikege ondu guriyiruttade.
hosa Uralli nelesuvudakkAgi, hosa kelasakke sEruvudakkAgi, illavE
Igina  kelasadallEnE  munde  hOguvudakkAgi  doDDavaru  hosa
dondu nuDiyannu kaliyatoDaguttAre. Adare cikkavareduru antaha
guriyiruvudilla.

hAgAgi, gurige takkudAda kalikeyannu doDDavarige odagisikoTTalli,
avaru adaralli bEgane munde hOgaballaru. ettugegAgi, avara
gurige Oduvudu mattu bareyuvudu mAtravE mukyavAgira bahudu;
hAgiddalli, mAtanADuvudakkintalU Oduvudakke mattu bareyuvudakke
avara kalikeyalli heccina ottu koDabEku.

doDDavarige yAvudE ondu viSayavannu tiLisabEkiddarU, adara
hindiruva kaTTalegaLannu tiLisuvudoLLeyadu. ettugegAgi, ingliSnalli
jiciNaheDi’s booYa ennuttEve Adare bDiciTichih oji Nahe NaDiee ennuttEve. ondu
kaDeyalli s emba oTTannu baLasalAguttade mattu innondu kaDeyalli
oji emba tunDupadavannu baLasalAguttade. Adare, kannaDadalli intaha
vyatyAsavilla; eraDu kaDegaLallU adaralli a emba ondE oTTannu
baLasalAguttade (tandeya pustaka, marada gellu).

ingliSgU kannaDakkU naDuviruva I vyatyAsavannu vivarisuvavaru
adara hindiruva kaTTaleyannU tiLisabahudu: ingliSnalli eraDu
hesaru(nAma)padagaLa  naDuvina  pattuge(sambanda)yannu  sUcisa
bEkAdAga, avu usirugara (jIvigaLa) pattugeyannu tiLisuvudAdare
sAmAnyavAgi s oTTannu baLasalAguttade, mattu bEre bageya pattuge
yannu  tiLisuvudAdare  oji  tunDupadavannu  baLasalAguttade.  I
vyatyAsada tiLivu ingliS kaliyuva doDDavarige neravAgaballudu.
kannaDadalli  esaka(kriyA)padagaLu  sollinalli  konege  baruttave;
Adare,  ingliSnalli  avu  naDuve  baruttave.  ettugegAgi,  keLagina
eraDu sollugaLannu hOlisi nODabahudu:

rAju manege hOda.

mEle koTTiruva kannaDada (1ka) sollinalli hOda emba esaka
pada sollina konege bandide; Adare ingliSna (1ca) sollinalli
tieTiNa emba esaka pada naDuve bandide.

kannaDadalli ondu hELikeyannu kELviyAgi mArpaDisabEkiddalli,
adara koneyalli baruva padakke O emba oTTannu sErisidare sAkAgu
ttade; Adare, ingliSnalli idakkAgi esaka padakke ondu ottAseya
padavannu sErisi, adannu sollina modala padavAgi baLasabEkAguttade,
mattu  A  sollinalli  bEreyU  kelavu  mArpADugaLannu  mADa
bEkAguttade.

nAyi bogaLitu.
nAyi bogaLitO?

kannaDa  mattu  ingliS  nuDigaLa  naDuve  intaha  halavAru
sollarimeya vyatyAsagaLive. ingliS sollugaLannu kaliyuttiruva
doDDavarige ivannu ettugegaLa mUlaka avara kalikeya angavAgi
tOrisikoDuttA hOdalli, avarige ingliS sollugaLannu Oduva
mattu  bareyuva  kelasagaLannu  naDesalu  heccu  suLuvAguttade.
yAkendare, avarige intaha tiLivannu tamma kalikeyalli baLasikoLLu
vantaha kasuvide.

7.3 eraDanE nuDiyAgi kannaDada kalike
eraDanE nuDiyAgi kannaDavannu kaliyabEkendiruvavarige, adarallU
mukyavAgi kannaDadalli Odalu mattu bareyalu tiLiyabEkendiruvavarige
kannaDada sollarimeya tiLivu neravige baraballudu. padagaLu nUlina
hAge, mattu sollarimeya kaTTalegaLu baTTeyalli kANisuva neygeya
hAge. nUlannu taratarada baTTegaLannAgi mArpaDisabEkiddare, mattu
adaralli hosa hosa cittAragaLannu mUDisabEkiddare hEge taratarada
nEygegaLa paricaya bEkAguttadeyO hAgeyE padagaLannu taratarada
sollugaLAgi jODisikoLLabEkiddarU sollarimeya kaTTalegaLa tiLivu
bEkAguttade.

sollugaLa  iTTaLa  entahadu  embudannu  tiLiyadavarige  avu
hEge  ondaroDanondu  sambandisive  embudannu  kanDukoLLalu
baruvudilla. heccina sollugaLallU esaka(kriyA)padavondiruttade,
mattu adu tiLisuva esakadalli pAlgoLLuva vyakti, vastu, viSaya
modalAduvannu  tiLisuva  hesaru(nAma)pada  illavE  padakante
gaLiruttave. ivannu gurutisaballavaru, mattu sollinalli baruva bEre

padagaLinda ivannu bErpaDisaballavaru Odinalli mattu baravaNigeyalli
yAvAgalU mundiruttAre.

sollugaLannu jODisuvudu hEge, ondu sollinoLage innondu
sollannu irisi hELuvudu hEge, tunDusollugaLannu padakanteyoLage
irisuvudu hEge embantaha viSayagaLannu tiLidukonDavarige tamma
barahavannu tiddi saripaDisalu heccu tondareyAguvudilla.

kannaDavannu kaliyuvavaru avara tAynuDiya sollarimegU kannaDada
sollarimegU naDuviruva mukyavAda vyatyAsagaLannu gamanisuva hAge
mADidalli, avara kalike innaSTu bEgane munduvariyaballudu. Adare,
idakkAgi kannaDaddE Ada sollarime entahadu embudannu kalisuvavaru
tiLidukonDirabEkAguttade.

kannaDadalli ivattu baLakeyalliruva sollarimeya (vyAkaraNada)
pustakagaLu  nijakkU  kannaDada  sollarime  entahadu  embudannu
tiLisuvudilla. hAgAgi, avugaLinda kannaDavannu eraDaneya nuDiyAgi
kaliyabEkendiruvavarige heccina neravu sigalAradu. tamiLu, telugu,
hindi, marATi modalAda bEre nuDigaLannADuvavarige kannaDavannu
kalisuvavaru avara tAynuDiya sollugaLigU kannaDada sollugaLigU
naDuve entaha vyatyAsagaLella ive embudannu gamanisabEku, mattu
avannu bEkAdAgalella kaliyuvavara gamanakke taruttirabEku.

I viSayadalli avarige neravAguvantaha hottagegaLannu sollarigaru
horatandalli innU oLLeyadu. nijakkU tamiLu, telugu, malayALa
modalAda kannaDakke tIra hattiraviruva (endare, ondE nuDikuTumbakke
sEriruva)  nuDigaLannADuvavarige  kannaDavannu  kalisuvalli  intaha
hOlikeya sollarimegaLu bEre bageyallU neravu nIDaballuvu.
ettugegAgi, tamiLu kannaDakke tIra hattirada nuDi. averaDara naDuve
heccu  kaDime  ondE  bageyavAgiruvantaha  halavAru  padagaLu,
padakantegaLu  mattu  sollugaLive.    tamiLarige  kannaDavannu  kalisa
bEkendiruvavaru  intaha  padagaLannu  mattu  sollugaLannu  baLasi
barahagaLannu baredalli, avannu kaliyuvavaru tumbA bEgane Odalu-
bareyalu kalitukoLLaballaru. idu avarige tamma kalikeya aLavina

mEle nambike huTTuvante mADaballudu, mattu idarindAgi avara
kalikeyU bEgane munde hOgaballudu.

7.4 tiruLu
eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli sollarimeya tiLivu yAva rItiyalli
neravige baraballudu embudannu I pasugeyalli pariSIlisalAgide.
I kalikeyannu modalanE nuDiya (tAynuDiya) taLahadiya mEle
naDesabEkAguvudAda kAraNa, modalanE mattu eraDanE nuDigaLa
naDuve sollarimeya kaTTalegaLalli entaha vyatyAsagaLella ive embu
dannu  tiLidukonDalli,  adu  avarige  innaSTu  heccina  neravannu
nIDaballudu.

eraDanE nuDiyannu kalisuva samayadalli tAynuDiyannu pUrti
horagiDabEkemba hELikege yAva AdAravU illa. nijakkU ingliS
taragatigaLalli makkaLa tAynuDiyannu baLasadiruvavaru doDDa tappu
mADuttiddAre.  yAkendare,  A  rIti  taragatiyalli  tAynuDiyannu
horagiTTarU makkaLa miduLinalli eraDanE nuDiya kalike A nuDiya
taLahadiya  mElEnE  naDeyuttade.  hAgAgi,  taragatiyallU
tAynuDiya taLahadiya mElEnE eraDanE nuDiyannu kalisuvudu
sariyAda dAri.

eraDanE nuDiya kalikeyalli tAynuDiya baLakeyinda tappugaLu
kANisuttave  emba  vAdavU  sariyalla.  yAkendare,  avu  nijakkU
kalikeya  hantagaLallade  tappugaLalla.  kalike  munduvaridante  avu
tAvAgiyE illavAguttave.

eraDanE nuDiyannu doDDavarige kalisuvavaru avara tAynuDigU
eraDanE nuDigU naDuve sollarimeyalli entaha hOlike mattu
vyatyAsagaLive embudannu gamanisuva hAge mADidalli, avara kalike
heccu bEgane munduvariyaballudu.

[English →](./29-kannaDa-vyAkaraNa-yAke-bEku-en#chapter-8--translation) | [Eke →](./29-kannaDa-vyAkaraNa-yAke-bEku-kn-eke#nuDimArike)

## enTanE pasuge — nuDimArike

8.1 munnOTa
ondu nuDiyalliruva barahavannu innondu nuDiya barahavannAgi
mArpaDisuvudakke kannaDaddE Ada nuDimArike emba padavannu illi
baLasalAgide.  I  kelasavannu  hesarisuvudakkAgi  samskruta  mUlada
bASAntara illavE anuvAda emba padavannu, mattu arEbik
mUlada tarjume emba padavannU kannaDadalli baLasalAguttade.

ondu  nuDiyalliruva  barahavannu  mAtravallade,  kelavomme
nEravAgi mAtannU bEre nuDige mArpaDisabEkAguttade. I kelasavannu
hesarisuvudakkAgiyU nuDimAru padavannE baLasabahudu. Adare,
I eraDu kelasagaLa naDuve kelavu vyatyAsagaLU ive. ingliSnalli
idakkAgi kelavomme TrAnsalET mattu inTarpreT emba eraDu
bEre bEre padagaLannu baLasuvudU ide.

barahagaLannu nuDimAruva samayadalli nuDimArugaru halavu
bageya  caLakagaLannu  baLasuttiruttAre.  Adare,  sAmAnyavAgi  ivu
avara arivige eTakada rUpadalliruttave. ivannu arivige eTakuva
hAge mADidalli, avaru I kelasavannu heccu cannAgi naDesikoDa
ballaru.

idallade, ellarigU intaha caLakagaLannu tAvAgiyE kalitukoLLalu
baruvudilla. yArAdarU tiLivigaru avannu kalisikoDabEkAguttade.
hAgAgi, oLLeya nuDimArugaru entaha caLakagaLannu baLasuttAre
embudannu  tiLidukonDu  avannu  uLidavarigU  kalisikoTTalli,
avarU oLLeya nuDimArugarAgaballaru.

nuDimArike

nuDimArikeyalli baLasabEkAgiruva caLakagaLalli halavu nuDiyarime
illavE sollarimeya tiLivannavalambisive. hAgAgi, avannu paDeyuvu
dakkAgi nuDimArugaru mUlanuDi mattu IDunuDigaLa sollarime
gaLannu  mAtravallade,  avugaLa  naDuviruva  vyatyAsagaLannU  tiLidira
bEkAguttade.  I  tiLivu  entaha  kaDegaLallella  neravige  baruttade
embudannu keLage (8.2-4)ralli vivarisalAgide.

nuDimArikegAgi  eNNuka(kampyUTar)gaLa  neravannu  paDeyuva
prayatnavannU kaLeda ayvattu varSagaLinda naDesalAguttide. nijakkU
nuDigaLa sollarime embudu eSTu toDakina viSaya emba sangati
intaha  prayatnadalli  toDagiruvavarige  tumbA  cannAgi  manavarike
yAgide. yAkendare, eNNukagaLige sollarimeya ondondu kaTTale
yannU  tiLisikoDabEkAguttade.  mUlanuDi  mattu  IDunuDigaLa
sollarimegaLannu mAtravallade avugaLa naDuvina vyatyAsagaLannU adakke
tiLisabEkAguttade. I kelasadalli tiLivigaru entaha sollarimeya
tondaregaLannella edurisabEkAguttade embudannu keLage (8.5)ralli
vivarisalAgide.

8.1.1 eraDu bagetagaLu
nuDimArikeya  kuritAgi  ivattu  tiLivigaralli  eraDu  bagetagaLive:
kelavara anisikeyante, ondu nuDiya barahavannu innondu nuDige
pUrtiyAgi nuDimAruvudu yAvattigU kaygeTukada kelasavE. idakke
avaru  koDuva  kAraNavEnendare,  ondu  nuDi  adannADuvavara
manassinalli ELuva anisikegaLannu innobbarige tiLisalu neravAguttade
mAtravalla,  avara  manassinalli  entaha  anisike  mUDaballudu
embudannU A nuDiyE tIrmAnisuttade.

nAvu paDeyuva tiLuvaLikegaLu illavE pADu(anubava)gaLu mattu
namma suttamuttalina parisarada kuritu namma manassinalli mUDuva
anisikegaLu  -  ivellavU  namma  nuDiyallE  unTAgabEkAgide.
hAgAgi,  nuDigaLa  naDuviruva  vyatyAsagaLu  avannu  ADuvavaru
paDeyabahudAda pADu, anisike, tiLivu - I mUrara  mElU

pariNAmagaLannu  bIradiruvudilla.  idarindAgi,  ondu  nuDiya
nnADuvavaru kANuva mattu paDuva prapanca innondu nuDiyannADu
vavaru  kANuva  mattu  paDuva  prapancakkinta  halavu  viSayagaLalli
bErAgiruttade.  hAgAgi,  ondu  nuDiya  mEle  avalambisiruva
anisike mattu tiLivugaLannu pUrtiyAgi innondu nuDiyalli nuDimAri
hELalu baruvudE illa embudAgi I tiLivigaru vAdisuttAre.

Adare  bEre  kelavu  tiLivigaru  idannu  oppuvudilla.  avara
anisikeyante, nAvu Enannu bEkiddarU namma nuDiyalli tiLisaballevu,
mattu avellavannU innondu nuDiyallU tiLisaballevu. nuDigaLa
naDuvina vyatyAsagaLella mElmayya vyatyAsagaLallade ALavAda vyatyAsa
gaLalla embudAgi avaru vAdisuttAre.

tiLivigara  naDuve  mUDiruva  I  tikkATakke  avaru  huruLu
(meciTiiTig) emba parikalpaneyannu baLasuvalli mADiruva tappu mUla
kAraNavendu nanage anisuttade. nijakkU illi tiLivu mattu huruLu
emba eraDu tIrA bErAgiruva parikalpanegaLu bEkAguttave. Adare,
avannu  hesarisuvudakkAgi  I  tiLivigaru  meciTiiTig  emba  ondE
padavannu baLasuva kAraNa, nuDimArikeya aLavina kuritu avaralli
mElina gondala unTAgide.

ondu padavannu kELidAga illavE OdidAga miduLinalli naragaLa
ondu  iTTaLa  mincuttade;  hAge  mincuvudE  A  padada  tiLivu.
hosa padavondannu tiLidukoLLuva samayadalli adannu kELidAga
illavE  OdidAga  mincaballantaha  naragaLa  iTTaLavondannu  namma
miduLalli hosadAgi unTAguttade. Adare, idu namma miduLinalli
naDeyuvantaha ondu Aguha mAtra. adannu nAvu namma mAtinalli
illavE Odinalli baLasikoLLaballevallade, adu nEravAgi namma arivige
eTakuvantahadalla.  adu  mincuvudannu  nODabEkiddare,  namage
upakaraNagaLa neravu bEkAguttade.

ellA padagaLigU intaha avugaLadE Ada tiLivugaLu iruttave;
yAkendare, yAva eraDu padagaLU namma miduLinalli naragaLa ondE
iTTaLa  mincuva  hAge  mADuvudilla.  kelavomme  namma  nuDiya

kuritu mAtanADuvAga, yAvudAdarondu padada tiLivu entahadu
embudannu innobbarige tiLisabEkAguttade. idannu hEge naDesuvudu?
idakkAgi nAvu ondu nEravallada dAriyannu kanDukonDiddEve:
ondu padada tiLivu entahadu embudannu innobbarige tiLisa
bEkAdAga,  antahadE  tiLivannu  koDuva  innondu  padavannu
baLasuttEve. ettugegAgi, kanikara emba padada tiLivEnu embudannu
innobbarige tiLisabEkAdAga, antahadE tiLivannu koDuva maruka
emba padavannu koDuttEve. nijakkU iveraDakke bEre bEre tiLivugaLu
iruttave.  hAgAgi,  maruka  embudannu  kanikara  padada  huruLu
embudAgi  kareyabahudallade  tiLivu  embudAgi  kareyalArevu.
idallade, bErondu kaDeyalli kanikara emba padavannu maruka padada
huruLAgiyU nAvu baLasaballevu.

maruka mattu kanikaragaLantaha eraDu padagaLige kannaDadalli ondE
huruLideyennuvudu avugaLalli ondannu innondara tiLiventahadu
embudannu sUcisuvudakkAgi baLasaballevu emba kAraNakkAgiyallade,
averaDU ondE tiLivannu koDuttave emba kAraNakkAgi alla. hAgAgi,
nuDiyondaralli  ondE  huruLina  (meciTiiTigna)  eraDu  padagaLu
iraballuvE emba viSayada kuritAgi tiLivigaroLage mUDibandiruva
tikkATakke  idE  tiLivu-huruLugaLa  naDuvina  vyatyAsavannu  avaru
gamanisadiruvudE kAraNa.

eraDu nuDigaLa padagaLannu hOlisi nODuvallU idE vyatyAsa
kANisikoLLuttade: ondu nuDiya padakke innondu nuDiya padavannu
huruLAgi koDaballevu. ettugegAgi, kannaDada maruka padakke ingliSna
chiomThicissioTi padavannu huruLAgi koDaballevu. Adare, maruka padada
tiLivu  ingliSna  chiomThicissioTi  padada  tiLivige  hattira  ideyallade
averaDU  ondE  alla.  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  I  eraDu  padagaLa
tiLivugaLu bErAgive.

ondu nuDiya barahavannu innondu nuDiya barahavAgi mArpaDisa
(nuDimAra) ballevE emba kELvi huruLu mattu tiLivugaLa naDuvina
I  vyatyAsavannavalambiside.  yAkendare,  ondu  nuDiya  sollige

heccukaDime antahadE tiLivannu koDuva innondu nuDiya sollannu
huruLAgi  koDaballevallade  pUrtiyAgi  adu  koDuva  tiLivannE
koDuva  sollannu  innondu  nuDiyalli  koDalArevu.  antaha
sollannu adE nuDiyallU koDalArevu!

8.1.2 nuDimAruva bage
ondu nuDiya barahavannu innondu nuDiya barahavAgi mArpaDisu
vudu suLuvAda kelasavEnalla. adannu meccugeyAguva hAge naDesalu,
A eraDu nuDigaLalli mAtanADalu mattu Odalu-bareyalu tiLididda
raSTE  sAladu.  avugaLa  naDuve  padagaLalli,  padarUpagaLalli,
sollarimeya kaTTalegaLalli mattu huruLugaLa nuDitadalli entaha
vyatyAsagaLive, I vyatyAsagaLu nuDimArikeyalli entaha tondaregaLa
nnoDDaballuvu  mattu  avannu  bageharisuvudu  hEge  embudannU
nuDimAruganu tiLidirabEkAguttade.

nuDimAruganige  bEkAguva  I  tiLivu  mukyavAgi  mUlanuDi
mattu IDunuDigaLa sollarimegaLinda, mattu averaDu sollarime
gaLannu hOlisi nODuvudarinda dorakuttade. ellA nuDigaLigU
avugaLadE Ada paricegaLiruttave. padagaLannu mattu padakantegaLannu
kaTTuva bage, avannu sollugaLalli baLasuva bage, tunDu sollugaLannu
sollugaLoLage irisuva bage, sollugaLannu jODisi kuraLu(pArA)
gaLannu  kaTTuva  bage,  sULunuDi(sambASaNe)gaLannu  bareyuva  bage
modalAdavugaLallella ondu nuDiya hAge innondu nuDi iruvu

I vyatyAsagaLannella gamanisikonDu, nuDimAruva samayadalli
mUlanuDiya paricegaLu IDunuDiya barahadoLage sErikoLLada
hAge  nODikoLLabEkAguttade.  yAkendare,  nuDiya  pariceyannu
badalAyisade uLisikoLLuva baraha mAtra sarAgavAgi OdisikonDu
hOguttade, mattu suLuvAgi tiLivannU koDuttade.

idallade,  barahagaLa  guriyannavalambisi  avugaLalli  bEre  bEre
bageya padagaLannu, sollina iTTaLagaLannu, mattu nuDigaTTugaLannu

baLasabEkAguttade.  prabandagaLalli  baLakeyAguva  pada  mattu
iTTaLagaLannE  jAhIrAtugaLallU  baLasidevAdare,  avu  tIrA
vicitravAgi kANisaballuvu. hAgAgi, barahada gurige hondikoLLuvante
tanna nuDimArikeyannu badalAyisikoLLuva caLakavU nuDimAruganigira
bEkAguttade.

intaha tiLivu mattu caLakagaLu nuDimAruganige yAke bEkAguttade
embudannu  ivattu  kelavu  kampenigaLa  jAhIrAtugaLalli  illavE
kaypiDigaLalli baruva kannaDa barahavannu nODidare gottAguttade.
I  barahagaLannu  nuDimArugarinda  baresuva  badalu  yAru
yArindalO  baresalAgide.  avarige  kannaDa  gottiruttade;  Adare,
nuDimAruvudu hEge embudu gottiruvudilla.

nuDimArugaru eraDu bageya tiLivugaLannu tamma kelasadalli baLasi
koLLabEkAguttade: mUla barahada guriyEnu, adara barahagArana
anisikegaLEnu, mUlanuDiyannu avanu yAva rItiyalli baLasikonDi
ddAne embudara tiLivu ondu bageyadu, mattu tAnu nuDimAruva
barahakke  entaha  OduganiddAne,  Atana  tiLivu  eSTara  maTTiginadu,
Ata Enannu edurunODuttirabahudu embudara tiLivu innondu
bageyadu.  I  eraDu  bageya  tiLivugaLannu  nuDimArugaru  hEge
baLasikoLLabahudu embudannu keLage vivarisalAgide:

8.2 mUla barahada tiLivu
mEle sUcisida hAge, barahada guri Enu embudannu tiLidukonDu,
adakke anusAravAgi tanna nuDimArikeyannu hondisikoLLalu nuDi
mAruganige gottirabEku. ettugegAgi, kate, kavite modalAdavugaLalli
barahagArara  anisikegaLige  heccina  ottu  koDabEkAguttade;  Adare,
varadigaLu,  prabandagaLu,  kalikeya  pustakagaLu  modalAdavugaLalli
barahagArara anisikegaLigintalU tiLivige heccina ottu koDabEkAgu
ttade.  jAhIrAtu,  rAjakIya  baraha,  manavi,  aDige  pustaka
modalAdavugaLalli ondu kelasavannu mADuva illavE innobbarinda
mADisikoLLuva bage hEge embudakke ottu koDabEkAguttade.

idallade, barahagaLalli yAva rItiya padagaLannu, padarUpagaLannu
mattu solliTTaLagaLannu baLasabahudu embudu, endare, barahada
oDDava entahadirabEku embudu adara guriyannavalambisiruttade.
suddihALegaLigAgi bareda barahakkU arivigarigAgi bareda barahakkU
naDuve intaha viSayagaLalli halavAru vyatyAsagaLiruvudannu gamanisa
bahudu.

barahada gurigaLa naDuviruva I eraDu bageya vyatyAsagaLannu
gamanisi,  avakke  anusAravAgi  tamma  nuDimArikegaLannu  hondisi
koLLuva aLavu nuDimArugarallirabEkAguttade. I eraDu kelasagaLannu
naDesuvallU sollarimeya tiLivu neravige baruttade.

8.2.1 ADunuDiya baLake
kelavu barahagaLalli mAtugaLannu bareyuvudakkAgi ADunuDiya baLake
yAgiruttade. ettugegAgi, kate-kAdambari, nATaka modalAdavugaLalli
intaha  baLakeyannu  kANabahudu.  kelavomme  samAjadalli  baLake
yalliruva  bEre  nuDigaLannU  baLasirabahudu.  intaha  barahavannu
nuDimAruvAga, IDunuDiya barahadallU ADunuDiyannu (mattu
bEre nuDigaLannu) baLasabEkE emba kELvi nuDimArugara eduru
nilluttade.

kelavondu kaDegaLalli ADunuDiya baLakeyannu nuDimArugaru
kaDegaNisabahudu. Adare, adara baLakege mUla barahadalli ondu
niScitavAda guriyideyAdare, adannu A rIti kaDegaNisuvudu sariyAga
lAradu.  hAgendu  IDunuDiya  barahadallU  adannu  kANisa
bEkendiddalli, nuDimArugaru halavu bageya toDakugaLannu edurisa
bEkAguttade.

barahagaLalli ADunuDigaLannu baLasuva bage mUlanuDiyalli baLake
yallirabahudu; Adare, IDunuDiyalli illadirabahudu. hAgiddalli,
tAnu hosadAgi antaha baLakeyannu IDunuDiyalli jArige tarabEkE
bEDavE embudannu nuDimArugaru tIrmAnisabEkAguttade.

mUla barahadalli ADunuDiyannu yAva guriyannirisikonDu
baLasalAgideyO adE guriyannu IDErisaballa ADunuDi IDu
nuDiyalli illadirabahudu. ettugegAgi, keLavargada janara ADunuDi
mUla barahada Odugaralli entaha anisikegaLannu huTTisuttadeyO
antahavE anisikegaLannu adu IDubarahadalli huTTisadirabahudu.
hAgiddalli, IDunuDiya barahadalli keLavargada janara ADunuDiyannu
baLasuvudarinda  mUlanuDiya  barahadalli  adakkidda  guri  IDEra
lAradu.

intaha kaDegaLalli nuDimArugaru ADunuDiyannu baLasuva badalu
bEre  yAvudAdarU  hammugeya  mUlaka  mUla  barahagArana
guriyannu IDErisalu prayatnisabEkAdItu. kelavaru barahagAraru
intaha kaDegaLalli IDunuDige tAvE ondu hosadAda ADunuDi
yannu kalpisikoLLuttAre.

tamma barahagaLalli ADunuDigaLannu baLasuvavaru sAmAnyavAgi
avannu pUrtiyAgi baLasuvudilla. yAkendare, hAge baLasidalli avara
baraha Odugarige gottE Agada hAge Agaballudu. hAgAgi, ADu
barahada saviyannaSTE Odugarige odagisuva hAge, kelavu padagaLannu
mattu padarUpagaLannu mAtra adarinda ArisikonDu, avannu avaru
tamma barahagaLalli baLasuttAre. nuDimArugaru idannu gamanisikonDu,
adakkanusAravAgi tamma nuDimArikeyallU ADunuDiya saviyannaSTE
odagisalu prayatnisabEku.

8.2.2 barahada oDDava
ondu barahavannu bareyuttiruva samayadalli barahagAraru halavu
bageya AykegaLannu naDesabEkAguttade: tammedurigiruva huruLannu
sUcisalu  eraDu  illave  heccu  padagaLiddalli,  avugaLallondannu
avaru ArisikoLLabEkAguttade; idE rItiyalli, tAvu tiLisabEkA
giruva sangatiyannu tiLisaballa solliTTaLagaLu halaviddalli, avugaLa
llondannu ArisikoLLabEkAguttade. barahagAraru naDesaballa intaha
AykegaLu  barahada  oDDavavannu  (Sayliyannu)  nirdarisuttave.

ondu barahadalli kANisuva oDDava barahagArana ALtana(vyaktitva)vannu
sUcisabahudu, illavE barahada bageyannU sUcisaballudu. ivannu
IDunuDiyallU kANisabEkE, mattu kANisuvudiddare adannu yAva
bageyalli kANisabahudu emba kELviyannu nuDimArugaru edurisa
bEkAguttade.

barahagArana  ALtanavannu  sUcisuvantaha  oDDavada  amSagaLu
sAmAnyavAgi  kate-kAdambarigaLantaha  nalbarahagaLalli  mAtra
kANisikoLLuttave. bEre bageya barahagaLalli avu kANisikoLLuvudu
aparUpa.  ettugegAgi,  arimeya  barahagaLalli  ellarU  baLasuva
oDDavavannE  barahagAraru  ArisikoLLuttArallade  tammadE  Ada
oDDavavannu baLasahOguvudilla. avugaLalli tiLivannu koDuvudara
mEle heccina ottu bILuvudu idakke kAraNavirabahudu.

mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  barahada  oDDavadalli  heccina  amSavU
adara guriyannu avalambisiruttade. ettugegAgi, makkaLigAgi bareda
barahakkU arivigarigAgi bareda barahakkU naDuve oDDavadalli halavu
vyatyAsagaLiruttave. arivigarigAgi bareda barahagaLalli sollugaLu heccu
aDakavAgiruttave, mattu avannu halaveDegaLalli hesaru padakantegaLAgi
badalAyisi, bEre sollugaLa angagaLAgi mADi baLasalAgiruttade.
Adare, makkaLigAgi bareda barahagaLalli ivondU iruvudilla. intaha
vyatyAsagaLannu  nuDimArugaru  gamanisikonDu,  IDu  barahadalli
avannu uLisikoLLalu prayatnisabEku.

idallade, ondE bageya solliTTaLa eraDu nuDigaLalli kANisi
konDAgalU, adannu yAke baLasalAguttade embudu nuDiyinda
nuDige  bErAgiraballudu.  ettugegAgi,  ingliS  nuDiya  pEsiv
(Thicissive)  iTTaLa  illavE  samskrutada  karmaNi  iTTaLakke  samanAgi
kannaDadalli paDu emba esakapadavannu baLasiruva kelasa mADalpaTTitu,
haNa koDalpaTTitu embantaha sollugaLannu kelavaru baLasuttAre.
Adare, I iTTaLada baLake kannaDadalli kelavE kelavu bageya barahagaLige
mAtra takkudAgide. hAgAgi, ingliSna pEsiv illavE samskrutada
karmaNi bandallella adannu kannaDadalli baLasalu baruvudilla.

8.2.3 bEre kelavu toDakugaLu
pada, padakante, sollugaLa iTTaLa modalAdavugaLa mUlaka tiLivannu
sUcisuva holabu(vidAna)gaLU nuDiyinda nuDige bErAgiruttave.
nuDigaLa naDuve kANisuva I vyatyAsagaLU nuDimArugarige tondare
koDuttave. oLLE nuDimArugaru I tondaregaLannu bageharisuvu
dakkAgi tammavE Ada upAyagaLannu kanDukonDiruttAre. hAgiddarU,
mUlanuDi mattu IDunuDigaLa naDuve entaha vyatyAsagaLella ive
embudannu paTTimADidalli, adu nuDimArugara kelasadalli heccina
neravannu koDaballudu.

mUlanuDiya padagaLige takkudAda padagaLu IDunuDiyalli illa
vAdalli, avakke badalu padakantegaLannu baLasuva illavE hosa pada
gaLannu unTumADikoLLuva aLavu oLLE nuDimArugarigiruttade.
mukyavAgi, omme bareda sollannu bage bageyAgi badalisikoLLuva
mUlaka adu Odugarige meccugeyAguva hAge mADuva aLavu
avarigiruttade. intaha kelasagaLalli sollarimeya arivu avara neravige
baraballudu.

ippuruLugaLiruva (ondakkinta heccu huruLugaLiruva) padagaLu
illavE sollugaLu mUlanuDiya barahadalli iveyAdalli, mUla
barahagArara manassinalli yAva huruLu iddirabahudu embudannu
UhisikonDu, adannu IDu barahadalli kANisabEkAguttade.

idallade, mUla barahadallillada ippuruLu IDu barahadalli
baLasabEkAguva  pada  illavE  sollinalli  kANisikoLLuvudAdare,
adarindAgi  Odugaralli  gondala  illavE  tapparimeyunTAgada
hAgeyU  nODikoLLabEkAguttade.  intaha  ippuruLugaLu
kANisadante nODikoLLalu baruvudiddare hAge mADuvudE oLLeyadu
(6.2 nODi).

ippuruLina pada illavE sollina iTTaLagaLa hAge, mUla baraha
dalli  kANisikoLLuva  mArpuruLu(rUpaka)gaLa  baLakeyU  nuDi
mArugarige tondare koDuttade. ettugegAgi, avanige taleyilla
emba sollinalli jANme illavE buddi padada badalu tale padavannu

ondu mArpuruLAgi baLasalAgide. I sollannu nuDimAruvAga,
IDunuDiyalli  antahadE  huruLannu  koDaballa  bEre  padavannu
illavE mArpuruLannu baLasabEkAguttade. tale padavannu hAgeyE
nuDimAridalli, takkudAda huruLannu adu IDunuDiya barahadalli
koDadE irabahudu.

mUla barahadalli baruva nuDigaTTugaLU nuDimArugarige tondare
koDuttave. avannu hAgeyE nuDimAralu baruvudilla. avu koDuva
huruLugaLannu  aritukonDu,  avannu  IDu  nuDiya  Odugarige
talapisuva kelasavannu nuDimArugaru naDesabEkAguttade. antahadE
tiLivannu koDuva bErondu nuDigaTTu IDu nuDiyalli ideyAdare,
adannU intaha kaDegaLalli baLasabahudu.

nuDimArugarige tondare koDuva innondu bageya padagaLendare,
mUlanuDiyalli  kaTTuniTTAda  huruLillada  padagaLu.  ettugegAgi,
cikkadu-doDDadu, oLLeyadu-keTTadu modalAda halavu padagaLige
kaTTuniTTAda huruLilla. IDunuDiyallU antahadE pada ideyAdare,
adannu baLasuva mUlaka tondareyannu bageharisabahudu.

Adare ellA kaDegaLallU hIge mADalu bAradirabahudu. ettuge
gAgi, nanTastikeyannu sUcisuva padagaLige ondondu nuDiyalli
ondondu  bageya  haravu  iruttade.  antaha  padagaLannu
nuDimAruvAga, mUlanuDiyalli nijakkU entaha nanTastikeyannu
sUcisalAgide  embudannu  tiLidukonDu,  adakke  samanAdantaha
IDunuDiya padavannu baLasabEkAguttade. kannaDada doDDamma emba
padakke badalAgi eTajaeDi moNaheDi embudannu baLasidalli adu ingliS
barahadalli hondikoLLalAradu.

8.3 IDunuDiya Oduga
ondu nuDimArida baraha cannAgideyendu hELabEkAdare, mUla
baraha adara Odugaralli entaha tiLivannu unTumADuttadeyO
antahadE tiLivannu nuDimArida baraha adara OdugarallU unTu
mADuvantirabEku.  I  ibbaru  Odugara  naDuve  halavu  bageya

vyatyAsagaLirabahudu.  ettugegAgi,  mUlanuDiya  Odugarigiruva
anubava illavE tiLivu IDunuDiya Odugarigiruva anubava illavE
tiLiviginta  tIra  bErAgirabahudu.  hIgiddalli,  mUla  barahavannu
nuDimAruvAga,  adaralli  halavu  bageya  badalAvaNegaLannU
nuDimArugaru mADikoLLabEkAguttade.

oLLeya nuDimArugaru AdaSTu maTTige tamma baraha Odugarige
suLuvAgi gottAguva hAge nODikoLLuttAre. kelavomme avaru
idakkAgi mUla barahadallilladiruva viSayagaLannU IDu barahadalli
hosadAgi  sErisikoLLuttAre.  nuDimArida  baraha  Odugarannu
dAritappisuvantirabAradu,  mattu  toDaku  toDakAda  pada  mattu
sollina iTTaLagaLa baLakeyinda Odugaru dUra hOguvanteyU
mADabAradu.

8.3.1 tiLidudu mattu tiLiyadudu
sollugaLige  iTTaLaviruva  hAge,  iDI  barahakkU  ondu  iTTaLa
viruttade. idu nuDiyinda nuDige bErAgiyU iruttade. hAgAgi,
mUla barahada iTTaLa entahadu embudannu tiLidukonDu, adakke
badalAgi antahadE huruLannu koDuva IDunuDiya iTTaLavannu
baLasaballavaru mAtra salIsAgi Odalu baruvantaha barahavannu bareya
ballaru.

ondu viSayada kuritu barahagArarige avara Odugariginta tusu
heccu gottiruttade. hAgAgi, barahagAraru tamma Odugarige gottiruvu
dannu modalige avara mundirisuttAre, mattu AmEle, avarige
gottilladudannu adakke sambandisiruva hAge tiLisuttAre. viSayagaLannu
paricayisuva I bageyannu heccina barahagaLallU kANabahudu.

barahagaLalli mAtravalla, sollugaLallU I tiLidudu-tiLiyadudu
vyatyAsavannu  kANabahudu.  ettugegAgi,  nimma  huDuga  nALe
baruttAne emba sollinalli nimma huDuga emba modalina amSa
tiLidudannu hELuttade mattu adara baLika baruva nALe baruttAne
emba amSa tiLiyadudannu hELuttade. idakke badalu, nALe baruvudu

nimma huDuga emba sollinalli nALe baruvudu embudE tiLidiruva
sangati. I kAraNakkAgi adannu sollinalli modalige baLasalAgide.
idannE nele-tiLivu vyatyAsa (3.2.1) sUcisuttade.

barahada mUlaka tiLisabEkAgiruva hosa (tiLiyada) viSayakke
ondu taLahadiyannodagisuvudakkAgi I rIti adaralli Odugarige
tiLidiruvantaha sangatiyannu modalige hELalAguttade. AmEleyU
Odugara Asaktiyannu barahadalli uLisikoLLuvudakkAgi, I holabannu
munduvarisalAguttade. idu hEgendare, modalige tiLiyadudAgidda
sangati,  adannu  tiLisidoDane,  tiLidudAguttade  mattu  I  tiLida
sangatiyannu  taLahadiyAgirisi,  bErondu  tiLiyada  sangatiyannu
Odugara mundiDalAguttade. tiLidudu mattu tiLiyadudu embavugaLa
naDuvina konDi I rIti barahaduddakkU tappade uLiyuva hAge
oLLE barahagAraru nODikoLLuttAre. antahavara barahada ondondu
sollinalli, kuraLinalli mattu pasugeyallU I konDi tappadiruttade.
oLLE Odugaru tAvu Oduttiruva barahadalli I rIti tiLidudu-
tiLiyadudu emba iTTaLavannu edurunODuttiruttAre. hAgAgi,
adannu baLasadiruva barahavannu avarige salIsAgi Odalu baruvudilla.
kelavomme  tiLiyadudannu  otti  hELuvudakkAgi  adannu  modalige
hELuvudU  ide.  Adare  idu  tumbA  aparUpavAgi  mAtra
baLasabEkAgiruva iTTaLa.

ondu nuDiya barahavannu innondu nuDige nuDimAruvAga,
adaralli  tiLidudu-tiLiyadudu  vyatyAsa  hEge  mUDibandide
embudannu  gamanisi,  IDu  barahadallU  adannu  uLisikoLLalu
prayatnisabEku. I viSayadalli mUlanuDi baLasuva holabiginta
IDunuDi  baLasuva  holabu  bEreyadAgiraballudAda  kAraNa,
nuDimArugaru I vyatyAsavannu gamanisuttirabEku.

8.3.2 hoddikeya gurutugaLu
hinde baredudakkU Iga bareyuttiruvudakkU naDuve yAva rItiya
hoddikeyide embudannu barahagAraru halavu bageya gurutugaLa

mUlaka sUcisuttiruttAre. intaha gurutugaLu nuDiyinda nuDige
bErAgiruvudarinda, mUla barahadalli baruva hoddikeya gurutu
gaLannu gamanisi, avakke badalAgi IDu nuDiyavE Ada gurutugaLannu
baLasalu oLLeya nuDimArugarige gottiruttade.

ettugegAgi,  ingliSnalli  hinde  hesarisiruva  vyakti  illavE
vastuvannu innomme sUcisabEkAdAga he, she, iNa modalAda tOru
padagaLannu baLasalAguttade. kannaDadalli I kelasakkAgi kelavu kaDegaLalli
avanu, avaLu, adu modalAda tOrupadagaLannu baLasabahu
dAdarU bEre kelavu kaDegaLalli tAnu padavannu baLasabEkAguttade.
idallade, kelavomme I padagaLu mUla barahadallilladiddarU
kannaDa barahadalli avannu baLasabEkAguttade, mattu kelavomme mUla
barahadalliddarU kannaDadalli avannu baLasadirabEkAguttade. nuDimAru
garu ingliS mattu kannaDa nuDigaLa naDuviruva I vyatyAsagaLannu
sariyAgi  tiLidukonDu,  bEkAgiruva  mArpADugaLannu  tamma
barahagaLalli mADikoLLabEkAguttade. illavAdare, avara barahadoLage
ingliS nuDiya parice nusuLibiDuttade.

8.4 nalbarahagaLa nuDimArike
kate, kavite, kAdambari, nATaka modalAda nalbarahagaLu nuDimArugarige
tammavE  Ada  bEre  kelavu  toDakugaLannu  tandoDDuttave.  avakke
huruLugaLu halavu maTTagaLalliruvudarinda, avannella tiLidukonDu
nuDimArida barahadallU avu kANisikoLLuvante mADuvudu suLu
vAda kelasavEnalla.

kelavara anisikeyante, kavanagaLannu nuDimAralu baruvudE illa.
avugaLalli huruLugaLu mattu uligaLu ondAgi hOguva kAraNa,
antahadE ondugUDuvikeyannu innondu nuDiyalli kalpisikoLLalU
baruvudillavembudAgi  avaru  hELuttAre.  hAge  kalpisikonDarU
adu bErondu kavanavAgaballudallade bErondu nuDiyalli baruva
adE kavanavAgalAradendu avaru vAdisuttAre.

bEre  kelavara  anisikeyante,  ondu  kavana  Odugaralli  entaha
pariNAmavannu  unTumADuttadeyO  antahadE  pariNAmavannu
unTumADaballa kavanavannu innondu nuDiyallU bareyaballevu.
Adare, idakke mUla nuDiya kavanavannu OdinODi, adara ALavAda
tiLivannu paDeyuva aLavu mAtravalla, antahadE tiLivannu koDuva
kavanavannu IDunuDiyalli bareyuva aLavU nuDimAruganige ira
bEkAguttade.  endare,  nuDimAruganu  orega(vimarSaka)nU  Agira
bEkAguttade, kaviyU AgirabEkAguttade.

idallade, ondu nuDiya mattu adannu baLasuva janara ELigege
A rIti bEre nuDigaLa kavanagaLannu mattu bEre bageya nalbarahagaLannu
nuDimAruvudu avaSya embudAgi avaru vAdisuttAre. yAkendare,
bEre nuDigaLalli nalbarahagAraru yAva rItiyalli tamma nuDiya
kasuvannu baLasikoLLuttAre mattu heccisikoLLuttAre embudannu intaha
nuDimArikegaLu tOrisikoDaballuvu.

8.5 eNNukada nuDimArike
barahavondannu ondu nuDiyinda innondu nuDige nuDimAralu
tumbA samaya tagaluttade. obba nuDimAruga ganTege aydAru
puTagaLannaSTE  nuDimArabahudu.  kelavu  bageya  barahagaLannu  Ata
svalpa bEgane mugisabahudu, Adare bEre kelavu bageya barahagaLannu
mugisalu Atanige innaSTu hottu tagalabahudu.

nuDimArabEkAgiruva barahagaLa eNike ivattu dinadinda dinakke
heccuttalE  hOguttide.  ingliSnantaha  nuDigaLinda  sAvirAru
barahagaLannu  bEre  nuDigaLige  nuDimAruttalE  irabEkAguttade.
koneyillada I kelasakke eSTu mandi nuDimArugariddarU sAkAguvu

hAgAgi, eNNuka(kampyUTar)gaLannu baLasuva mUlaka I kelasavannu
heccu bEgane mattu kaDime veccadalli naDesabahudallavE embudAgi
halavaralli Asakti mUDiddu, kaLeda ayvattu varSagaLinda I viSayadalli
arake(samSOdane)gaLu naDeyuttive. idaralli svalpa maTTige geluvU

avarige doretideyendu hELabahudu. ganTege nUrinnUru puTagaLaSTu
barahagaLannu ivattina eNNukagaLu nuDimArikoDaballuvu.

Adare, eNNukagaLu nuDimAri koDuva I barahagaLalli halavu
tappugaLu uLidiruttave. avannella nuDimArugaru kayyindalE tiddi
saripaDisabEkAguttade. idakke mukya kAraNavEnendare, nuDimAruva
samayadalli nAvu naDesabEkAgiruva halavu kelasagaLalli kelavannu
naDesalu eNNukagaLige sAdyavE Aguvudilla. kelavu bageya barahagaLa
maTTigantU I rIti eNNukaLu koDuva nuDimArikeyannu tiddalu
hOguvudakkintalU nEravAgi mUla barahavannu nuDimAruvudE
suLuvAda kelasavendu kelavarige anisuttade.

hIgiddarU, eNNukagaLa mUlaka nuDimAruva kelasavannu nAvu
ivattu naDesalEbEkAgide. iduvarege inTarneTnalli heccina viSaya
gaLU ingliSnallE kANisikoLLuttidduvu. hAgAgi, ingliS nuDi
gottiddare, namage bEkAdudannella inTarneTnalli paDeyabahudemba
anisikeyittu.

Adare,  ittIcege  adaralli  bEre  nuDigaLa  baLake  heccuttA
hOguttide. ettugegAgi, japAnina inTarneT nelegaLalli heccinavU
japAnIs nuDiyallE ive. hAgAgi, inTarneT mUlaka heccu
heccu viSayagaLannu tiLiyabEkendiruvavaru illavE heccu heccu
janarannu  avugaLa  mUlaka  talupabEkendiruvavaru  ingliS  nuDi
yondannE nambikonDiddare sAladu.

inTarneTnalli ondakkinta heccu nuDigaLalli bandiruva viSaya
gaLannu tiLiyabEkendiruvavarige eNNukada nuDimArike neravige bara
balludu. ettugegAgi, ingliSninda kannaDakke nuDimAruva ErpADu
inTarneTnallE ideyAdare, adannu baLasi ingliSnalliruva yAva
barahavannu  bEkiddarU  nEravAgi  A  ErpADina  mUlaka  kannaDakke
mArpaDisi Odalu ingliS tiLiyada kannaDigarigU sAdyavAgabahudu.
idallade, intaha bEre halavu nuDigaLalliruva barahagaLannu kannaDakke
nuDimAruvantaha  ErpADugaLannu  inTarneTnalli  aLavaDisi
konDevAdare, avugaLalli yAva nuDiyalliruva barahavannu bEkiddarU

ellA kannaDigarU kannaDadallEnE inTarneTnalli Odi tiLidukoLLalu
baruvavante mADaballevu.

modamodalige intaha eNNukagaLa mUlaka nAvu paDeyaballa
nuDimArikegaLu  tumbA  tappugaLinda  kUDiddu,  oraToraTAgira
bahudu. Adare, intaha oraToraTAda nuDimArikegaLindalU namage
neravannu paDeyalu baruttade. yAkendare, ivattu inTarneTnalli
nAvu huDukuva barahagaLalli heccinavU tiLivige sambandisidavu. oraTu
nuDimArikegaLu intahadondu barahadalli entaha tiLivu sigaballudu,
adu  namage  bEkAgiruvantahadE  allavE  embaSTannAdarU  tiLisa
balluvu. adu bEkAgiruvantahadendu gottAda mEle bEkiddare,
nuDimArugara neravininda adara oLLeya nuDimArikeyannu paDeyalu
hOgabahudu.

8.5.1 eNNukada hammugegaLu
nuDimArikege eNNukavannu baLasatoDagida samayadalli, adara mUlaka
ondu nuDiya barahavannu innondu nuDige nEravAgi nuDimAra
bahudemba  anisike  tiLivigarallittu.  barahadalli  baruva  padagaLannu
ondondAgi  innondu  nuDige  badalAyisidalli,  mattu  avannu
sollugaLAgi jODisuva kramadalli kelavu mArpADugaLannu mADi
konDalli, adu A innondu nuDiya barahavAgaballudu embudAgi
avaru bAvisiddaru. ingliS mattu raSyan nuDigaLa naDuve intaha
eNNukada nuDimArikeyannu naDesalu kelavu prayatnagaLannU naDesa
lAyitu.

Adare,  intaha  prayatnagaLannu  kaygettikonDAga  halavAru
toDakugaLu kANisikonDuvu. mukyavAgi, sollugaLa iTTaLaventahadu
embudannu tiLidukoLLade ondu nuDiya sollugaLannu innondu
nuDiya  sollugaLAgi  nuDimAralu  baruvudillavemba  viSaya  I
prayatnagaLinda  gottAyitu.  hAgAgi,  AmElina  prayatnagaLallella
mUla nuDiya barahadalliruva padagaLannu IDunuDiya padagaLondige

hondisuvudarondige mUla barahadalliruva sollina iTTaLagaLannU
IDunuDiya iTTaLagaLondige hondisalAguttide.

eNNukagaLu barahagaLannu nuDimArabEkiddalli avakke halavu bageya
arivu  bEkAguttade.  barahadalli  baLakeyAguva  padagaLige  entaha
huruLugaLella ive embudannu avu aritirabEku, mattu idakkAgi
avugaLalli padanerakegaLirabEku. padagaLu sollugaLalli hEge baLake
yAguttave, mattu hAge baLakeyAguvAga avugaLa halavu huruLu
gaLalli ondu hEge AykegoLLuttade embudannu avu aritirabEku,
mattu idannu avakke tiLisaballa sollarimeya kaTTalegaLu avugaLalli
irabEku.

barahagaLalli baruva padagaLa huruLu avannu baLasiruva kuLLiha
(sandarba)da mElU avalambisiruttade. mAnavana miduLu I vyatyAsa
vannu  suLuvAgi  aritukonDu,  kuLLihakke  hondikeyAguvantaha
huruLannu  suLuvAgi  AydukoLLaballudu.  Adare,  I  kelasavannu
naDesalu  bEkAguva  arivannu  eNNukagaLige  koDisuvudu  hEge
embudinnU tiLivigarige gottAgilla. hAgAgi, I viSayadalli eNNuka
gaLu tumbA tappu mADuttive.

8.5.2 mAreDe hammuge
ivattu  nuDimAruva  kelasakkAgi  eNNukagaLalli  mukyavAgi  eraDu
bageya hammugegaLannu baLasalAguttade. ivannu mAreDe hammuge
mattu eDenuDi hammuge embudAgi kareyabahudu. ivugaLalli
modalaneyadannu baLasuvavaru tiLivannu nEravAgi mUlanuDiyinda
IDunuDige mAreDegoLisu(vargAyisu)ttAre, mattu eraDaneyadannu
baLasuvavaru tiLivannu modalige ondu kalpitavAgiruva eDenuDige
mAreDegoLisi, allinda IDunuDige mAreDegoLisuttAre.

mAreDe  hammugeyalli  mUru  hantagaLiruttave:  modalaneya
hantadalli  mUla  barahada  huruLEnu  embudannu  kanDuhiDidu,
adannu mUlanuDiyadE Ada ondu kalpita rUpakke badalAyisa
lAguttade;  eraDaneya  hantadalli  adannu  antahadE  Ada  ondu

IDunuDiya  kalpita  rUpakke  mAreDegoLisalAguttade;  mattu
mUraneya  hantadalli  IDunuDiya  I  kalpita  rUpavannu  adara
baraharUpakke mArpaDisalAguttade.

mUla barahada huruLannu kanDuhiDiyalu modalaneya hantadalli
adara sollugaLannu biDisinODalAguttade. adaralli baLakeyAgiruva
padagaLu  entahavu  (hesarupadagaLE,  esakapadagaLE  illavE
sollarimege  sambandisida  padagaLE),  avannu  yAva  huruLinalli
baLasalAgide,  barahadalli  baruva  sollugaLa  iTTaLa  entahadu,
ippuruLina  iTTaLaviruva  sollugaLannu,  nuDigaTTugaLannu  illavE
mArpuruLu(rUpaka)gaLannu  baLasalAgideyAdare  avu  entaha
huruLugaLalli  baLakeyAgive  embantaha  halavAru  viSayagaLannu
tIrmAnisikoLLuva kelasavannu I hantadalli naDesabEkAguttade.

I  rIti  mUla  barahada  padagaLu,  sollarimeya  iTTaLagaLu,
mattu averaDara mUlaka huruLugaLannu gurutisiruva bage - ivannella
biDisiTTAga, A barahada kalpita rUpavondu doreyuttade.

eraDaneya hantadalli mUla barahada I kalpita rUpavannu IDu
barahada kalpita rUpakke mArpaDisalAguttade. idakkAgi, mUlanuDigU
IDunuDigU naDuve padagaLalli, sollina iTTaLagaLalli, mattu avugaLa
mUlaka huruLugaLannu gurutisuva bageyalli entaha vyatyAsagaLella
iveyO avannella baLasikoLLabEkAguttade.

mUraneya hantadalli IDu barahada I kalpita rUpavannu adara
nijavAda  baraha  rUpakke  mArpaDisalAguttade.  esaka  padagaLige
himbottannu (bUtakAlavannu) illavE mumbottannu (baviSyatkAla
vannu) tiLisuva padarUpagaLannu koDuvudu, hesarupadagaLige avugaLa
pAngugaLannu  gurutisuva  annu,  inda,  ge,  mattu  alli  emba
oTTugaLalli ondannu sErisuvudu, hesarupadagaLigU esakapadagaLigU
naDuve hondANikeyannu unTumADuvudu modalAda kelasagaLannu
I hantadalli naDesalAguttade.

I  mUru  hantagaLige  bEkAguva  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi
eNNukakke  mUru  bageya  padanerakegaLannu  odagisabEkAguttade:

mUlanuDiya padarUpagaLa, sollarimeya mattu huruLugaLa tiLivannu
koDuva padanerake; IDunuDiya kuritAgi antahadE tiLivannu koDuva
innondu padanerake; mattu I eraDara naDuvina pattuge(sambanda)
yannu tiLisuva mUraneyadondu innuDiya padanerake.

eNNukagaLige odagisabEkAgiruva I viSayagaLannu mUru bEre
bEre angagaLalli odagisalAguttade. ettugegAgi, modalaneya hantakke
bEkAguva  viSayagaLannu  pada  mattu  padarUpakke  sambandisidavu,
sollarimege  sambandisidavu,  mattu  huruLugaLige  sambandisidavu
embudAgi mUru angagaLalli bErpaDisi koDalAguttade.

idE rItiyalli, eraDanE mattu mUranE hantagaLige bEkAguva
viSayagaLannU mUru bEre bEre angagaLalli bErpaDisi koDalAgu
ttade. hIge mADuvudarindAgi, munde avugaLalli mArpADugaLannu
mADikoLLuva kelasa heccu suLuvinadAguttade.

8.5.3 eDenuDi hammuge
mAreDe hammugeginta eDenuDi hammuge sollugaLige kalpita rUpavannu
koDuvalli mAtra bErAgiruttade. mUlanuDiya barahavannu adaradE
Ada kalpita rUpakke mArpaDisuva badalu, I hammugeyalli adannu
ondu eDenuDige (kalpitavAgiruva nuDige) mArpaDisalAguttade.

hIge mADuvudarinda siguva prayOjanavEnendare, AmEle I
eDenuDiyinda bEre yAva nuDige bEkiddarU barahavannu nuDimAra
bahudu. ettugegAgi, kannaDada ondu barahavannu eDenuDiya baraha
vAgi mArpaDisidalli, AmEle adannu nEravAgi tamiLu, telugu,
malayALa, hindi modalAda bEre halavu nuDigaLalli yAvudara
barahavAgi bEkiddarU mArpaDisikoLLabahudu. idakke badalu, mAreDe
hammugeyalli ondondu nuDijODigU nuDimAralu bEkAguva
kelasagaLannella bEre bErAgi mADikoLLabEkAguttade.

jagattina ellA nuDigaLigU samAnavAgabahudAdantaha, endare
yAvudE ondu nuDiya pariceyannU baLasadiruvantaha eDenuDi

yondannu unTumADaballevu emba huccu utsAha I eDenuDi
hammugeyannu havmikoLLalu horaTidda tiLivigarallittu. Adare samaya
kaLedantella, idu talapalAgada guri embudu spaSTavAguttide.

ettugegAgi, mUla barahadalli kANisuva ellA bageya ippuruLu
gaLannU intaha eDenuDiyalli bageharisikoLLabEkAguttade. Adare,
idannu naDesuvudu aSTondu suLuvina kelasavEnalla. yAkendare,
bEre bEre nuDigaLa naDuve bEre bEre bageya pada mattu iTTaLagaLa
ippuruLugaLu kANisikoLLuttave. hAgAgi, nAvu kalpisabEkAgiruva
eDenuDiyannu jagattina ellA nuDigaLondigU hOlisi nODade
adaralli kANisaballa ippuruLugaLannella mEle sUcisida hAge bage
harisalu baruvudilla.

 intaha halavu toDakugaLu mAreDe hammugeyalli illavAguttave.
ettugegAgi, adara modalanE hantadalli mUlanuDige sambandisi
dantaha  ippuruLugaLannu  mAtra  bageharisidare  sAku;  IDunuDige
sambandisidantaha  ippuruLugaLEnAdarU  uLididdare,  avannu
mAreDegoLisuva eraDanE hantadalli bageharisabahudu.

idallade, mUlanuDigU IDunuDigU naDuve kANisuva halavu
bageya  hOlikegaLannu  mAreDe  hammugeyalli  nAvu  baLasikoLLa
ballevu; averaDara naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLannu mAtra nAvu bageharisi
koLLabEkAguttade. Adare, eDenuDi hammugeyalli nuDigaLa naDuve
kANisikoLLaballa  ellA bageya vyatyAsagaLannU bageharisikoLLabEkAgu
ttade.  yAkendare,  adu  ellA  nuDigaLigU  samAnavAgiruvantaha
amSagaLannaSTE  oLagoLLabEkAgiruttade.  I  kAraNakkAgi,  eDenuDi
hammugeyalli tumbA toDaku toDakAda sollarimeya kaTTalegaLannu
unTumADikoLLabEkAguttade.

ivattu eDenuDi hammugegaLannu baLasuvavaralli heccinavarU kelavE
kelavu  nuDigaLige  samAnavAgiruvantaha  eDenuDigaLannu  mAtravE
kalpisikoLLuttAre. ettugegAgi, yurOpina nuDigaLa naDuve nuDi
mAruvudakkAgi unTumADiruvantaha eDenuDi allina nuDigaLige
mAtra  samAnavAgideyallade  bEre  nuDigaLige  samAnavAdudalla.

hIge mADuvudarinda avaru kalpisikoLLabEkAgiruva eDenuDi heccu
toDakinadAguvudilla.

8.5.4 eNikeya hammuge
mElina eraDu bageya hammugegaLigU neravAguva hAge, innondu
bageya hammugeyannU kelavaru tiLivigaru hammikonDiddAre. idaralli
IgAgalE unTumADiruva nuDimArikegaLannu baLasikoLLuvantaha
aLavannu eNNukagaLige koDisalAguttade.

I  aLavina  neravininda,  eNNukagaLu  eraDu  nuDigaLa  naDuve
IgAgalE naDesiruva nuDimArikegaLalli ondu nuDiya pada, pada
rUpa,  sollina  iTTaLa  modalAdavugaLige  badalAgi  innondu
nuDiyalli yAva pada, padarUpa, sollina iTTaLa modalAduvu
heccineDegaLallU  baLakeyAguttave  embudannu  kanDukoLLuttave,
mattu I viSayavannu nenapinallirisikonDu, antahavE Ada pada,
padarUpa,  sollina  iTTaLa  modalAduvannu  bEkAdAga  baLasuva
aLavannu tAvE unTumADikoLLuttave.

ettugegAgi, ingliS mattu phranc nuDigaLa naDuve halavAru
barahagaLannu IgAgalE nuDimAralAgide. I barahagaLalli yAva
mUlanuDiya  padagaLige  badalAgi  yAva  IDunuDiya  padagaLu
ati  heccu  kaDegaLalli  baLakeyAguttave  embudannu  eNNukagaLu
gamanisikoLLuttave. hosadAgi barahavondannu ingliSninda phranc
nuDige illavE phrancninda ingliS nuDige nuDimArabEkAdAga,
I  eNNukagaLu  ondondu  padakkU  samanAgiruva  padagaLalli  A
rIti tumbA heccu bAri baLakeyAgiruva padavannE ArisikoLLuttave,
mattu  idarindAgi,  avu  naDesuva  nuDimArike  Odugarige  heccu
meccugeyAguva hAgAguttade.

Adare, I hammugeyannu baLasabEkiddalli sAvirAru irnuDiya
barahagaLu eNNukagaLige sigaballa rUpadalli irabEkAguttade. hAgAgi,
sadyakkantU I hammugeyannu ingliS, phranc, jarman modalAda
kelavE kelavu nuDigaLalli mAtra baLasaballevu.

8.5.5 eNNukagaLa toDakugaLu
nuDimAruvalli eNNukagaLu halavu bageya toDakugaLannu edurisa
bEkAguttade. avugaLalli kelavannu hammugegaLalli badalAvaNegaLannu
mADuva mUlaka bageharisabahudu; Adare bEre kelavannu sadyakkantU
bageharisalArevendE hELabEkAguttade. eNNukagaLu koDuva baraha
vannu  nuDimArugarinda  tiddisuva  mUlakavEnE  intaha  toDaku
gaLindAgi mUDibaruva tappugaLannu saripaDisabEkAguttade.

barahagaLalli kANisikoLLuva ippuruLugaLu sAmAnyavAgi Odugarige
yAva tondareyannU koDuvudilla. yAkendare, avarige sollu
gaLannu baLasiruva kuLLiha(sandarba)dinda, illavE tamma anubavadinda
sariyAda huruLannu ArisikoLLalu baruttade. Adare, eNNukagaLige
avu tumbA tondare koDuttave. yAkendare, kuLLihada tiLivannu
eNNukagaLige koDisuvudu hEge embudinnU tiLivigarige gottAgilla.
idallade, eNNukagaLige padagaLa huruLannu gamanisalu baruttadallade
avugaLa tiLivannu gamanisalu baruvudilla (8.1.1 nODi). hAgAgi,
mUlanuDiya barahadalli kANisuva pada mattu sollugaLa huruLu
entahadu embudannu mAtravE avu baLasikoLLaballuvallade, nEravAgi
pada mattu sollugaLu Odugaralli mUDisuvantaha tiLivu entahadu
embudannu avu baLasikoLLalAravu.

mEle sUcisida hAge, padagaLa tiLivannu avugaLa huruLugaLu
pUrtiyAgi koDalAravu. yAkendare, eraDu padagaLa naDuve tiLivinalli
tusuvAdarU vyatyAsa iddE iruttade. hAgAgi, ondu padavannu
innondu padada huruLAgi koDuvAgalella intaha tiLivina vyatyAsa
gaLannu kaDegaNisuttalE irabEkAguttade. ellA nuDigaLigU samAnavAga
balla eDenuDiyondannu unTumADuvalli idU ondu toDakAgide.

8.5.6 oLanuDigaLa nuDimArike
kelavu  arime(vijnAna)gaLige  mattu  paLagikegaLige  sambandisidante
avugaLavE  Ada  oLanuDigaLu  beLedu  bandiruttave.  ettugegAgi,

kOrTugaLige  sambandisidante  oLanuDiyondu  baLakege  bandiddu,
kOrTina  barahagaLallella  adara  baLakeyAguvudannu  kANabahudu.
idE rItiyalli halavu bageya arimeya (vijnAnada) barahagaLallU
avugaLadE Ada oLanuDigaLu baLakeyAguttiruttave. I rIti tammadE
Ada ondu oLanuDiyannu baLasuva barahagaLannu eNNukagaLa mUlaka
nuDimAruvudu heccu suLuvAda kelasa.

yAkendare, intaha barahagaLallella ondu bageya viSaya mAtra
baruttadeyAda  kAraNa,  avugaLalli  baLakeyAguva  padagaLa  eNike
dinabaLakeya nuDiyalli baLakeyAguva padagaLa eNikeginta tumbA
kaDime  iruttade.  idallade,  I  padagaLige  kaTTuniTTAda  huruLU
iruttade.  hAgAgi,  eNNukagaLige  I  barahagaLalli  baruva  padagaLa
huruLugaLannu kanDuhiDiyalu heccu tondareyAguvudilla.

intaha  barahagaLalli  kelavE  kelavu  sollina  iTTaLagaLu  mAtra
baruttiruttave.  hAgAgi,  avugaLannu  nuDimAralu  bEkAguva
sollarimeya tiLivannu eNNukagaLige koDisalu heccu tondareyAguvu
dilla. dinabaLakeya nuDiyalli bAradiruvantaha kelavu iTTaLagaLU
ivugaLalli baLakeyAguttirabahudu. Adare, ivu A oLanuDiya ellA
barahagaLallU baruva kAraNa, avugaLindalU heccu tondareyAguvu

idallade, nuDigaTTugaLu mattu mArpuruLina padagaLu illavE
padakantegaLu intaha barahagaLalli baLakeyAguvudu tumbA kaDime.
Adare, sollarimeya mArpuruLugaLu heccu baLakeyAguttave. hAgAgi,
avannu  sollugaLondige  sambandisuva  bageyannu  eNNukagaLige
tiLisabEkAguttade.

I ellA kAraNagaLigAgi, oLanuDiyalli barediruva barahagaLannu
nuDimAruvudakkAgi  eNNukagaLannu  baLasikoLLuvudu  dinabaLakeya
nuDiyalli barediruva barahagaLannu nuDimAruvudakkAgi baLasikoLLuvu
dakkinta heccu suLuvAda kelasavAgide. idallade, eNNukagaLu koDaballa
nuDimArikegaLu oLanuDiyavAgiddalli, avu heccu mandi Odugarige
meccugeyAgaballuvu.

8.5.7 eNNukagaLigAgi bareyuvudu
eNNukagaLa toDakannu kaDime mADalu nammedurigiruva innondu
upAyavendare,  avugaLige  nuDimAralu  suLuvAguva  hAge
barahavannu  tiddi  bareyuvudu,  illavE  bareyuvAgalEnE  avakke
anukUlavAguva hAge bareyuvudu. ettugegAgi, ellA rAjyagaLigU
kaLisikoDabEkAgiruva ondu varadiyannu bareyuvAgalEnE eNNuka
gaLige anukUlavAguva hAge baredalli, adannu nEravAgi, mattu
heccuna  OdugarigU  meccugeyAguva  hAge  eNNukagaLa  mUlaka
nuDimAri AyA rAjyagaLige kaLisikoDabahudu.

ondu baraha eNNukagaLige anukUlavAgabEkiddalli, adaralli cikka
cikka sollugaLannu baLasirabEku; heccu uddavAgiruva mattu sikkalu
sikkalAgiruva  sollugaLannu  baLasirabAradu;  adaralli  baruva
sollugaLella  sollarimeya  kaTTalegaLige  anusAravAgirabEku;
hELabEkAgiruvudannu aDakavAgi hELirabEku; avaSyavillada padagaLannu
mattu eNNukakke tiLidillada padagaLannu baLasirabAradu; mattu AdaSTu
maTTige  ippuruLina  padagaLu  mattu  iTTaLagaLu  adaralli  bArada
hAge nODikoLLabEku.

intaha barahagaLannu eNNukagaLu Odugarige meccugeyAguva hAge

nuDimAraballuvu.

8.6 tiruLu
barahagaLannu ondu nuDiyinda innondu nuDige nuDimAra bEkendiru
vavarige sollarimeya tiLivu halavu bagegaLalli neravige baraballudu.
mUla  nuDiya  sollarimeyannu  mAtravallade  IDunuDiya
sollarimeyannU avaru idakkAgi tiLidirabEkAguttade. ADunuDi
illavE oLanuDigaLannu baLasiruva barahagaLannu nuDimArabEkiddalli,
IDunuDiyalli  baLakeyAguttiruva,  mattu  avakke  samanAgiruva
ADunuDi  illavE  oLanuDigaLa  sollarimeyannU  avaru  tiLidira
bEkAguttade.

eNNukagaLa  mUlaka  barahagaLannu  nuDimArabEkiddalli  avakke
mUlanuDi  mattu  IDunuDigaLa  sollarimeyannu  tiLisikoDa
bEkAguttade; hAgAgi, antaha kelasagaLannu naDesuvavarU I eraDu
nuDigaLa  sollarimegaLannu  innaSTu  heccu  vivaravAgi  tiLidira
bEkAguttade.

<a id="adhyAya-9"></a>

[English →](./29-kannaDa-vyAkaraNa-yAke-bEku-en#chapter-9--language-planning) | [Eke →](./29-kannaDa-vyAkaraNa-yAke-bEku-kn-eke#nuDihammuge)

## ombattanE pasuge — nuDihammuge

9.1 munnOTa
nuDigaLu kAladinda kAlakke mArpaDuttA iruttave. haLegannaDaviddaddu
naDugannaDavAgi, ivattu hosagannaDavAgi mArpaTTide; ondu kAladalli
kannaDavemba ondE nuDiyiddudu ivattu soligara kannaDa, havyaka
kannaDa, maysUru kannaDa, hubbaLLi kannaDa modalAda ADunuDigaLAgi,
illavE kannaDa mattu baDaga emba eraDu nuDigaLAgi bErpaTTide.

I rIti kannaDa nuDi mArpaDalu, mattu halavu ADunuDigaLAgi
illavE nuDigaLAgi bErpaDalu adaralli baLakeyAguttiruva uligaLalli,
padagaLalli  mattu  sollarimeya  iTTaLagaLalli  kAladinda  kAlakke
mArpADugaLu naDeyuttiruvudu, mattu I mArpADugaLu bEre
bEre UrugaLalli mattu jAtigaLalli bEre bEre rItiyalli naDeyu
ttiruvudu mukya kAraNa.

intaha mArpADugaLu nuDiya oLagannu tAguva badalu adara
iruvikeyannU tAgaballudu. ondu nuDi illadAgabahudu, illavE
hosadondu  nuDi  mUDibarabahudu.  ettugegAgi,  ondu
nuDiyannADuva janaralli ellarU sAvannappidalli, illavE ellarU
adannu  biTTukoTTu  bErondu  nuDiyannu  baLasatoDagidalli,  A
nuDiyE illadAgabahudu.

halavu nuDigaLu berakegonDu avugaLinda hosa nuDiyondu
mUDibarabahudu. ettugegAgi, halavu nuDigaLannADuva janaru oTTige
vAsamADabEkAdAga, A ellA nuDigaLa amSagaLannU oLagonDiruva
berakenuDiyondu avara naDuve baLakege baruttade, mattu cikkandinalli

nuDihammuge

antaha nuDiyannu kELuttA beLeyuva makkaLa bAyiyalli adondu
hosa nuDiyAgi mArpaDuttade.

9.1.1 mArpADugaLu yAke naDeyuttave?
nuDigaLalli  kANisikoLLuva  mArpADugaLalli  heccinavU  yAke
naDeyuttave embudu namage gottAguvudilla. ettugegAgi, haLegannaDa
dallidda pakAra hakAravAgide, ra-Ra mattu La-ZagaLa naDuvina vyatyAsa
illavAgide, allagaLeyuva rUpa badalAgide (haLegannaDadalli mADan
endiddudu ivattu hosagannaDadalli mADalikkilla endAgide); intaha
mArpADugaLella kannaDadalli yAke naDedive embudannu nAvu vivarisa
lArevu.

Adare,  nuDigaLalli  kANisikoLLuva  bEre  kelavu  mArpADugaLu
avannADuva janara hosa hosa bEDikegaLannu neravErisuvudakkAgi
naDeyuttave. ettugegAgi, samskruta, ingliS modalAda bEre nuDi
gaLinda kannaDakke halavAru padagaLu eravalAgi bandive; ivugaLalli
halavu kannaDigara bALveyalli hosadAgi sErikonDiruva vastugaLannu
illavE viSayagaLannu hesarisuvudakkAgi bandive.

hosagannaDada halavu ADunuDigaLalli ondu ADunuDi barahada
nuDiyAgi mattu ellara nuDiyAgi ivattu baLakege bandiruvudU
hIgeyE kannaDigara bEDikeyondannu neravErisuvudakkAgi naDediruva
mArpADu. barahada nuDiyAdudarindAgi adaralli AmEle bEreyU
halavu  mArpADugaLu  naDeyabEkAyitu,  mattu  I  mArpADu
gaLindAgi adu ivattu mUla ADunuDiginta halavu viSayagaLalli
bErAgide.

sAmAnyavAgi, intaha mArpADugaLu ADugara bEDikegaLannanusarisi
nuDigaLalli naDeyuttalE iruttave. avannu yArU nuDiya mEle
hEruvudilla. idakke badalu, ondu nuDiyalli entaha mArpADugaLu
naDeyabEku embudannu ondu kUTa, ondu ADaLita illavE obba
vyakti tIrmAnisi, adarante avannu naDesalu toDagabahudu, mattu

adakkAgi kaTTaLe illavE kAnUnugaLannu mADabahudu. idannu illi
nuDihammuge endu kareyalAgide.

nuDiya  baLakeyalli  samAjavu  edurisuva  toDakugaLannu
bageharisuvudakkAgi nuDihammugegaLannu kaygettikoLLalAguttade. ettuge
gAgi, halavu nuDigaLiruva ondu nADinalli ellarigU ondE Agiru
vantaha nuDiyondu illadirabahudu. I korateyannu hOgalADisu
vudakkAgi, ADaLita ondu kAnUnannu mADabahudu, mattu antaha
kAnUnina mUlaka, baLakeyalliruva halavu nuDigaLalli ondu nuDi
ellara  nuDiyAgi,  endare  SAleya,  ADaLitada  mattu  barahada
nuDiyAgi baLakege baruvante mADabahudu.

 ondu nuDiyalli hosadAgi barahavannu beLesabEkendiruva janaru,
adakkiruva halavu ADunuDigaLalli yAvudAdarU ondannu Arisi
konDu,  adaralli  barahagaLannu  unTumADalu  toDagabahudu.
samaya kaLedante, A ADunuDi barahada nuDiyAgi nelegoLLabahudu.
ondu nuDiya barahadalli barige(akSara)gaLa toDakugaLu (spelling
samasyegaLu) halavirabahudu; ettugegAgi, adaralli baLakeyAguva
barigegaLigU barahavannu Oduva bagegU naDuve sariyAda hondANike
yilladirabahudu.  idarindAgi,  A  nuDiya  barahavannu  kaliyuva
mattu baLasuva kelasa tumbA toDakinadAgirabahudu. I toDakannu
illavAgisuvudakkAgi, antaha barigegaLannu biTTukoDabEkemba tIrmAna
vannu vyaktiyobbanu baLakege tarabahudu, mattu Atana tIrmAnavannu
bEre barahagAraru oppikoLLabahudu.

I rIti ADaLita, kUTa, illavE vyaktigaLu naDesuva nuDihammugegaLa
mUlakavU ondu nuDiya illavE ADunuDiya parice(rUpa) mattu
baLakegaLalli naDeyabEkAgiruva mArpADugaLu naDeduhOgaballuvu.

9.1.2 hammugegaLa bagegaLu
mEle sUcisida hAge, mArpADugaLu nuDiya oLagannu tAgabahudu,
illavE  adara  iruvikeyannU  tAgabahudu.  idakkanusAravAgi,

nuDihammugegaLU eraDu bageyavAgiraballuvu. avugaLa guri nuDiya
oLagannu mArpaDisuvudAgirabahudu, illavE adara iruvikeyalli
mArpADugaLannu taruvudAgirabahudu.

nuDiya  oLagannu  tAguva  hammugegaLa  mUlaka  hosa  hosa
kelasagaLannu  naDesuvalli  adannu  baLasalu  baruva  hAge  nAvu
mADaballevu. ettugegAgi, ondu nuDiyannu kOrTu kacErigaLalli
illavE  SAle-kAlEjugaLalli  baLasabEkiddalli,  adakke  bEkAguva
sAvirAru heccina padagaLu A nuDiyallirabEkAguttade. nuDihammugeya
mUlaka ivannella unTumADikoTTalli antaha baLake suLuvAguttade.
nuDiya iruvikeyannu tAguva hammugeya mUlaka samAjadalli
baLakeyalliruva halavu nuDigaLalli ondara bele uLidavugaLa beleginta
heccAguva  hAge  mADabahudu.  ettugegAgi,  halavu  nuDigaLalli
ondannu kalikeya illavE ADaLitada nuDiyAgi ArisikonDalli, adara
bele  heccuttade;  samAjadalli  adara  baLakeyU  heccu  haravannu
paDeyuttade: heccu heccu mandi adannu baLasuvantAguttade.

I  eraDu  bageya  hammugegaLu  ondakkondu  sambandisive
embudannu  gamanisuvudu  avaSya.  ettugegAgi,  ondu  nuDiyalli
arimeya (vijnAnada) kalikege bEkAguva sAvirAru hosa padagaLannu
unTumADikoTTiddarU, A nuDiyannu antaha kalikegAgi baLasalu
toDagadiddalli, avu padanerake(kOSa)gaLalli mAtravE kANisikoLLuva
padagaLAgi uLiyaballuvallade A nuDiya padagaLendenisalAravu.

9.1.3 hammugeya hantagaLu
I eraDu rItiya nuDihammugegaLannU nAlku mukya hantagaLa mUlaka
baLakege tarabEkAguttade. ivannu Ayke, parice, baLake mattu beLavaNige
embudAgi hesarisabahudu.

ettugegAgi, barahavannu baLasadiruva nuDiyondannu barahakkiLisa
bEkemba nuDihammuge namma mundirabahudu. idakkAgi, modalige
yAvudAdarondu lipiyannu ArisikoLLabEkAguttade. idu rOman

lipiyirabahudu, nAgari lipiyirabahudu, illavE parsO-arEbik
lipiyirabahudu.

eraDaneyadAgi, A lipiyalliruva barige(akSara)gaLalli yAvuvannu
baLasabEku mattu yAvuvannu biDabEku, avugaLa mUlaka nuDiya
uligaLannu illavE padagaLannu hEge sUcisabEku, nuDiyalliruva
heccina uligaLannu sUcisalu entaha heccina barigegaLu bEkAguttave,
avannu hEge unTumADikoLLabEku embantaha halavAru tIrmAna
gaLannu  kaygoLLabEkAguttade.  I  tIrmAnagaLu  A  nuDiyalli
baLasabEkAgiruva lipige adaradE Ada ondu pariceyannu koDuttave.
mUraneyadAgi, I lipiyannu baLakege taruva kelasa naDeyabEku.
idannu obba vyakti naDesabahudu, kelavaru barahagAraru oTTu sEri
naDesabahudu  illavE  kAnUnugaLa  mUlaka  ADaLitavU  adannu
naDesaballudu. SAlegaLa kalikeyalli adannu sErisuva mUlaka, mattu
dinapatrike,  vArapatrikegaLalli  mattu  pustakagaLalli  adannu  baLasuva
mUlaka, heccu heccu janaralli adu baLakega baruva hAge mADa
bahudu.

nAlkaneyadAgi, baLakege tandiruva I lipiyalli halavu rItiya
beLavaNigegaLu naDeyabEkAguttade: bEre bEre kaDegaLalli baLasuvu
dakkAgi  adara  barigegaLannu  dappabarige,  teLubarige,  mAlubarige
modalAda halavu oDDavagaLalli unTumADabEkAguttade; adannu
beraLaccu  mADalu  adara  barigegaLannu  kIlimaNeyalli  aLavaDisa
bEkAguttade;  eNNuka(kampyUTar)gaLalli  baLasalu  tantrAmSagaLannu
unTumADabEkAguttade.

nuDihammugeya I nAlku hantagaLalli eraDu mattu nAlkanE
hantagaLannu naDesabEkiddalli, adakke sollarimeya tiLivu bEkAguttade.
antaha  tiLivilladavaru  avannu  naDesahOgi,  hEge  samAjavannu
halavAru bageya tondaregaLalli silukisiddAre embudannu gamaniside
vAdare, idu yAke bEku embudu gottAguttade.

nuDiya hammugege sollarimeya tiLivu yAke bEku embudannu
tOrisikoDuvudE I pasugeya guriyAda kAraNa, parice mattu

beLavaNige emba adara eraDu mattu nAlkaneya hantagaLannu mAtra
illi gamanisalAgide.

9.2 parice hammuge
ondu  nADinalli  illavE  samAjadalli  nuDihammugeya  mUlaka
entaha mArpADugaLannu naDesabEku embudannu mukyavAgi sAmAjika
neleyalli naDesalAguttade. ettugegAgi, isrElnalli baLakeyallidda
halavu nuDigaLalli hIbrU nuDiyannu ellara nuDiyAgi ArisikoLLa
lAyitu mattu adannE ADaLita, kAnUnu, kalike modalAdavugaLalli
baLasuva tIrmAnavannu mADalAyitu. isrElnalli nelesida janaralli
heccinavarU  yehUdigaLAgiddudE  I  rIti  hIbrU  nuDiyannu
ArisikoLLalu mukya kAraNa.

ondu nuDi illavE ADunuDiyannu ellara nuDiyAgi mArpaDisa
bEkiddalli,  adara  pariceyalli  halavu  bageya  mArpADugaLannu
mADikoLLabEkAguttade;  adannu  barahadalli  baLasuttillavAdalli,
adakkondu lipiyannu koTTu barahakke iLisabEkAguttade; adannu
halavu mandige hosadAgi kalisabEkAguttadeyAda kAraNa, hAge
kalisalu bEkAguva sollarimeyondannu tayArisabEkAguttade; mattu,
adannu halavu bageya hosa hosa kelasagaLalli baLasabEkAguttade
yAda kAraNa, A kelasagaLige bEkAguva halavAru hosa padagaLannu
adaralli unTumADabEkAguttade.

intaha nuDipariceya mArpADugaLannu sariyAgi, munde janarige
tondareyAgada hAge, naDesabEkiddalli, adannu naDesikoDuvavaru
nuDiyarimeyannu  mattu  A  nuDiya  sollarimeyannu  cannAgi
tiLidirabEkAguttade.

9.2.1 barigehammuge
barahavillada nuDige ondu hosa lipiyannu aLavaDisuvudu, mattu
